lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	萊哈曼兄弟走下 , 整個大崩潰 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	在俄羅斯 , 非洲的農場有火 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在都深深地深深地深深地互相連結 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	意思是 , 一個國家獨立和其他人合作 , 沒有與其他人合作 , 而不是與他人合作 , 而非與他人合作 , 而非與他人合作 , 而非與他人合作 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為在國內國家的行動 , 國家本身也沒有效率 , 因為在國內國家的影響會發生在他們身上 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是一位年輕士兵 , 當時是英國的年輕士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我的國家有多強大 , 我們的軍隊有多強 , 我們的軍隊有多強 , 我們的軍隊 , 我們的力量 , 強大的力量是如何強大的 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	當敵人在牆壁中被外圍牆壁 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人在牆壁中 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 我想談談我的國家 , 我得說 , 對安全來說 , 我的國家 , 要談談我的國家 , 我得說 , 對安全來說 , 我的國家 , 要談談防禦 , 我得說 , 農業 , 因為流行病是一種威脅 , 我必須說 , 農業 , 因為流行病是一種威脅 , 我必須說 , 在我的國家 , 公共衛生部門 , 我們要談談防禦 , 我必須說 , 農業 , 因為流行病是一種威脅 , 我必須說 , 對安全來說 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談談 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談談 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談談 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談談 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談話 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我得和國內部長談話 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我得說的是 , 我必須說 , 在我國內 , 我們要談談我的國家 , 我得說的是 ,
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	它不再是美國國家的安全性 , 一個國家的安全只是一個國家的安全 , 只是一個國家的安全 , 一個國家的安全 , 只是一個國家的安全 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	它的能力可以鎖在一起 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴你一件很重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴你們 , 我們的政府 , 在工業革命的經濟模式上 , 建構了 , 建立在工業革命的經濟模型上 , 實際上 , 政府 , 基本上 , 建構了整個工業革命的經濟模型 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你在商業知道 , 我們的典型結構 , 是網路 。
it's your capacity to network that matters , both within your governments and externally .	它是你的能力 , 網際網路 , 都在你的政府和外面 。
so here is ashdown's third law .	這是三條法律 。
by the way , don't ask me about ashdown's first law and second law because i haven't invented those yet ; it always sounds better if there's a third law , doesn't it ?	順帶一提 , 別問我先生的第一條法律和第二條法律 , 因為我沒有發明 , 但它總是聽起來更好 , 如果有第三個法律 , 不要問我 。
ashdown's third law is that in the modern age , where everything is connected to everything , the most important thing about what you can do is what you can do with others .	第三條法則是 , 在現代年齡中 , 最重要的事情是你能和其他人一起做的事 。
the most important bit about your structure whether you're a government , whether you're an army regiment , whether you're a business is your docking points , your interconnectors , your capacity to network with others .	最重要的是 , 你的社交網絡 , 不管你是企業 , 你的關係 , 你的關係 , 你的網絡 , 你的關係 。
you understand that in industry ; governments don't .	你知道在產業中 , 政府不行 。
but now one final thing .	但 , 最後一件事 。
if it is the case , ladies and gentlemen and it is that we are now locked together in a way that has never been quite the same before , then it's also the case that we share a destiny with each other .	假如 , 女士們 , 先生們 , 我們與彼此之間的差距是相同的 。
suddenly and for the very first time , collective defense , the thing that has dominated us as the concept of securing our nations , is no longer enough .	突然間 , 第一次 , 集體防禦 , 已經把我們視為一個概念 , 來保護我們的國家 , 不再夠 。
it used to be the case that if my tribe was more powerful than their tribe , i was safe ; if my country was more powerful than their country , i was safe ; my alliance , like nato , was more powerful than their alliance , i was safe .	總體來說 , 我是安全的 , 如果我的國家比他們的國家更強大 , 我是安全的 , 我是安全的 , 我是安全的 , 我是安全的 。
it is no longer the case .	它不再是這樣 。
the advent of the interconnectedness and of the weapons of mass destruction means that , increasingly , i share a destiny with my enemy .	與敵人之間的關係 , 與敵人之間的關係 , 與敵人之間的差距很大 。
when i was a diplomat negotiating the disarmament treaties with the soviet union in geneva in the 1970s , we succeeded because we understood we shared a destiny with them .	我在1970年代 , 在1970年代 , 我們成功了 , 因為我們了解我們與他們共享 , 我們成功了 。
collective security is not enough .	集體安全並不足夠 。
peace has come to northern ireland because both sides realized that the zerosum game couldn't work .	和平已經來到北京 , 因為兩邊都意識到 , 和平是零和平 。
they shared a destiny with their enemies .	他們和敵人的敵人有敵人 。
one of the great barriers to peace in the middle east is that both sides , both israel and , i think , the palestinians , do not understand that they share a collective destiny .	在中東地區最棒的障礙之一就是兩邊 , 兩邊 , 我認為 , 巴勒斯坦人 , 不了解他們共享集體 。
and so suddenly , ladies and gentlemen , what has been the proposition of visionaries and poets down the ages becomes something we have to take seriously as a matter of public policy .	突然間 , 女士們先生們 , 女士們先生們 , 我們必須認真是公共政策的重要性 。
i started with a poem , i'll end with one .	我從一首詩開始 , 我會結束 。
the great poem of john donne's .	約翰•唐納的一首詩 。
" send not for whom the bell tolls . "	「 別忘了貝殼 。 」
the poem is called " no man is an island . "	這首詩叫做 「 沒有人是島嶼 。 」
and it goes: " every man's death affected me , for i am involved in mankind , send not to ask for whom the bell tolls , it tolls for thee . "	它會說: 「 每個人的死亡都會影響我 , 每人死亡都會影響我 , 不論是誰是貝殼 , 都會影響我 。 」
for john donne , a recommendation of morality .	約翰•唐納 , 是道德的建議 。
for us , i think , part of the equation for our survival .	對我們來說 , 我認為 , 人類生存的一部分 。
to find the path to long life and health , dan buettner and team study the world's " blue zones , " communities whose elders live with vim and vigor to recordsetting age . at tedxtc , he shares the 9 common diet and lifestyle habits that keep them spry past age 100 .	為了找到一條路徑 , 長壽命、丹佛頓和世界的 「 藍色區塊 」 , 他們在tedxttner和團隊研究這個世界: 「 藍色區塊 」 , 在tedxttner和團隊研究世界的 「 藍色區塊 」 , 他們在tedxttner和團隊研究這個世界: 「 藍色區塊 」 , 在tedxttner和團隊研究世界的 「 藍色區塊 」 , 每一百歲都在tedxtner 。
biology , culture , exploration , food , health , life , science	生物學、文化、探索、食物、健康、生命 。
dan buettner: how to live to be 100+	danbuett:如何活到100+ 。
something called the danish twin study established that only about 10 percent of how long the average person lives , within certain biological limits , is dictated by our genes .	一個叫做dndneddneddneddneddneddneddneddneddned的研究 , 只佔了人類生命中有10%的長壽命 , 在某些生物限制中 , 我們的基因有多長 。
the other 90 percent is dictated by our lifestyle .	另外百分之九十的人被我們的生活型態 。
so the premise of blue zones: if we can find the optimal lifestyle of longevity we can come up with a de facto formula for longevity .	所以 , 藍色區塊:如果我們能找到最佳的生活方式 , 我們就可以找到最適合的生命方式 。
but if you ask the average american what the optimal formula of longevity is , they probably couldn't tell you .	但如果你問平均美國人最樂觀的平均壽命 , 他們可能無法告訴你 。
they've probably heard of the south beach diet , or the atkins diet .	他們可能聽過南海灘飲食 , 或皮膚飲食 。
you have the usda food pyramid .	你有美國食物金字塔 。
there is what oprah tells us .	歐普拉告訴我們 。
there is what doctor oz tells us .	醫生奧茲告訴我們 。
the fact of the matter is there is a lot of confusion around what really helps us live longer better .	重點是 , 有很多困惑 , 可以讓我們更活得更好 。
should you be running marathons or doing yoga ?	你應該要跑馬拉松或做瑜伽嗎 ?
should you eat organic meats or should you be eating tofu ?	你應該吃肉食 , 或應該吃肉嗎 ?
when it comes to supplements , should you be taking them ?	當它到供應時 , 你應該要拿他們嗎 ?
how about these hormones or resveratrol ?	這些荷爾蒙或逆轉性呢 ?
and does purpose play into it ?	目的是要玩樂嗎 ?
spirituality ? and how about how we socialize ?	精神性 ? 我們如何社會化 ?
well , our approach to finding longevity was to team up with national geographic , and the national institute on aging , to find the four demographically confirmed areas that are geographically defined .	我們的研究方式是與國家地理協調合作 , 找到了四個人口統計資料 , 來找到四個人口統計資料 , 來找到四個人口統計數據 。
and then bring a team of experts in there to methodically go through exactly what these people do , to distill down the crosscultural distillation .	接著 , 把各式各樣的團隊專家們 , 去了解這些人如何做 , 將跨越跨越文化的分裂 。
and at the end of this i'm going to tell you what that distillation is .	最後我要告訴各位 , 發生了什麼 。
but first i'd like to debunk some common myths when it comes to longevity .	但首先 , 我想要破壞一些常見的迷思 , 來延長壽命 。
and the first myth is if you try really hard you can live to be 100 .	第一個迷思是 , 如果你嘗試真的很難你可以活到100歲 。
the problem is , only about one out of 5 , 000 people in america live to be 100 .	問題是 , 只有15000人在美國生活中只有1分之一 。
your chances are very low .	你的機會非常低 。
even though it's the fastest growing demographic in america , it's hard to reach 100 .	即使是美國最快成長的人口統計數字 , 很難達到100 。
the problem is that we're not programmed for longevity .	問題是 , 我們不是程式要長壽 。
we are programmed for something called procreative success .	我們被稱為 「 成功 」 的成功 。
i love that word .	我喜歡這個詞 。
it reminds me of my college days .	它提醒了我大學 。
biologists term procreative success to mean the age where you have children and then another generation , the age when your children have children .	生物學家說: 「 年齡 」 , 當你孩子的孩子有小孩時 , 你的孩子就有小孩了 。
after that the effect of evolution completely dissipates .	進化後的效果完全消失了 。
if you're a mammal , if you're a rat or an elephant , or a human , in between , it's the same story .	如果你是哺乳動物 , 如果你是哺乳類動物 , 或人類 , 相同的故事 。
so to make it to age 100 , you not only have to have had a very good lifestyle , you also have to have won the genetic lottery .	所以 , 要讓它變成一百歲 , 你不只需要擁有一個非常好的生活方式 , 你也必須有好的生活方式 。
the second myth is , there are treatments that can help slow , reverse , or even stop aging .	第二個迷思是 , 治療可以幫助緩慢、逆轉 , 或甚至停止 。
when you think of it , there is 99 things that can age us .	當你想到它時 , 有99個東西可以用我們 。
deprive your brain of oxygen for just a few minutes , those brain cells die , they never come back .	把你的腦細胞死掉 , 幾分鐘後 , 大腦細胞死亡 , 它們從來沒有回來 。
play tennis too hard , on your knees , ruin your cartilage , the cartilage never comes back .	玩樂團很困難 , 你膝蓋的膝蓋 , 沒有回來 。
our arteries can clog . our brains can gunk up with plaque , and we can get alzheimer's .	我們的藝術家可以克服 , 我們可以得到阿茲海默症 。
there is just too many things to go wrong .	很多事情都錯了 。
our bodies have 35 trillion cells , trillion with a " t . " we're talking national debt numbers here .	我們的身體有35兆個細胞 , 叫做 「 t 」 , 我們在說國家債務 。
those cells turn themselves over once every eight years .	這些細胞自從每八年開始 。
and every time they turn themselves over there is some damage . and that damage builds up .	每當他們把自己丟到某個損傷後 , 就會產生傷害 。
and it builds up exponentially .	而且它建構出了數量 。
it's a little bit like the days when we all had beatles albums or eagles albums and we'd make a copy of that on a cassette tape , and let our friends copy that cassette tape , and pretty soon , with successive generations that tape sounds like garbage .	有點像是垃圾 , 我們都有一陣子彈 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快地 , 讓朋友複製 , 很快就成功了 。
well , the same things happen to our cells .	同樣的事發生在我們的細胞 。
that's why a 65yearold person is aging at a rate of about 125 times faster than a 12yearold person .	這是為什麼65倍的速度比十二歲的人還快十二歲 。
so , if there is nothing you can do to slow your aging or stop your aging , what am i doing here ?	所以 , 如果沒有任何東西可以緩慢你的衰退 , 或停止你 , 我在做什麼 ?
well , the fact of the matter is the best science tells us that the capacity of the human body , my body , your body , is about 90 years , a little bit more for women .	最重要的是最好的科學告訴我們 , 身為女性 , 我的身體 , 你的身體 , 你的身體 , 大概90年來 , 最重要的是最好的科學 。
but life expectancy in this country is only 78 .	但在這個國家只有78歲 。
so somewhere along the line , we're leaving about 12 good years on the table .	在這條線上 , 我們留下了12個好年 。
these are years that we could get .	這些年來 , 我們就能得到 。
and research shows that they would be years largely free of chronic disease , heart disease , cancer and diabetes .	研究顯示 , 大部分的疾病、心臟病、癌症、糖尿病、心臟病、癌症及糖尿病 。
we think the best way to get these missing years is to look at the cultures around the world that are actually experiencing them , areas where people are living to age 100 at rates up to 10 times greater than we are , areas where the life expectancy is an extra dozen years , the rate of middle age mortality is a fraction of what it is in this country .	我們認為最好的方法之一就是去看世界各地的文化 , 人們生活在這個國家中年齡的數年 , 比我們所預期的還要多十年 , 平均壽命率高達10倍 。
we found our first blue zone about 125 miles off the coast of italy , on the island of sardinia .	我們發現我們的第一個藍色區塊是西元1125英里的東京 。
and not the entire island , the island is about 1 . 4 million people , but only up in the highlands , an area called the nuoro province .	不是整個島嶼 , 島上有1400萬人 , 但只有在高島 , 島上有1.4萬人 。
and here we have this area where men live the longest , about 10 times more centenarians than we have here in america .	這裡有這個地區 , 美國的人口活得比我們還要多 。
and this is a place where people not only reach age 100 , they do so with extraordinary vigor .	這是一個地方 , 人們不只到達100歲 , 他們也做得很好 。
places where 102 year olds still ride their bike to work , chop wood , and can beat a guy 60 years younger than them .	102歲的年輕人 , 比起他們騎腳踏車去工作 , 可樂隊 , 比他們更年輕 。
their history actually goes back to about the time of christ .	他們的歷史其實是回到基督教的 。
it's actually a bronze age culture that's been isolated .	其實是一片垃圾文化 , 被孤立 。
because the land is so infertile , they largely are shepherds , which occasions regular , lowintensity physical activity .	因為土地是相同的 , 它們大大是羊群 , 體積極大 。
their diet is mostly plantbased , accentuated with foods that they can carry into the fields .	他們的飲食主要是植物 , 只能用食物來做 , 以致於它們能攜帶的食物 。
they came up with an unleavened whole wheat bread called carta musica made out of durum wheat , a type of cheese made from grassfed animals so the cheese is high in omega3 fatty acids instead of omega6 fatty acids from cornfed animals , and a type of wine that has three times the level of polyphenols than any known wine in the world .	他們出發了一首詩歌 , 一名叫卡達卡塔音樂 , 由沙發來製造出來的 , 由動物組成的 , 而一種風力 , 一種風力 , 一種風力 , 一種風力 , 一種風力 , 比任何任何已知的葡萄酒所產生的三倍之多 。
but the real secret i think lies more in the way that they organize their society .	但真正秘密我認為謊言是他們組織社會的秘密 。
and one of the most salient elements of the sardinian society is how they treat older people .	sardinian社會中最嚴重的之一就是他們如何治療老年人 。
you ever notice here in america , social equity seems to peak at about age 24 ?	你們注意到美國 , 社會平等似乎是24歲時嗎 ?
just look at the advertisements .	看看廣告 。
here in sardinia , the older you get the more equity you have , the more wisdom you're celebrated for .	在沙丁尼亞 , 老年人有更多的智慧 , 更有智慧 , 你就會得到更多智慧 。
you go into the bars in sardinia , instead of seeing the sports illustrated swimsuit calendar , you see the centenarian of the month calendar .	你在沙丁尼亞看過運動 , 看運動會穿透鏡片 , 看運動是月球表達的運動 。
this , as it turns out , is not only good for your aging parents to keep them close to the family it imparts about four to six years of extra life expectancy research shows it's also good for the children of those families , who have lower rates of mortality and lower rates of disease .	結果證明 , 對於這些家庭而言 , 不只好對孩子們來說 , 還能給父母保持住家 , 更低率的死亡率和低率的死亡率 , 和低率的死亡率 。
that's called the grandmother effect .	這叫做 「 祖母效果 」 。
we found our second blue zone on the other side of the planet , about 800 miles south of tokyo , on the archipelago of okinawa .	我們發現我們的第二個藍色區域 , 大約800英哩 , 南方西班牙 , 北京 , 北京 。
okinawa is actually 161 small islands .	okinawa是161個小島 。
and in the northern part of the main island , this is ground zero for world longevity .	而在北極的北部地區 , 這是地球的一部分 。
this is a place where the oldest living female population is found .	這裡是最古老的居住女性族群 。
it's a place where people have the longest disabilityfree life expectancy in the world .	它是一個地方 , 人們在世界上最長壽命的生命期待 。
they have what we want .	他們有我們想要的 。
they live a long time , and tend to die in their sleep , very quickly , and often , i can tell you , after sex .	他們活了很長的時間 , 很快地 , 通常 , 我可以告訴你 , 死亡在睡眠中 , 很快地 , 通常 , 我可以告訴你 ,
they live about seven good years longer than the average american .	他們比平均壽命的七年長 。
five times as many centenarians as we have in america .	美國有五倍 。
one fifth the rate of colon and breast cancer , big killers here in america .	第五分之一的乳癌、乳癌 , 大殺人在美國 。
and one sixth the rate of cardiovascular disease .	心血管疾病的四分之一 。
and the fact that this culture has yielded these numbers suggests strongly they have something to teach us .	這些數字建議很強烈地告訴我們 。
what do they do ?	他們會怎麼做 ?
once again , a plantbased diet , full of vegetables with lots of color in them .	再一次 , 一個植物的飲食 , 有許多顏色的蔬菜 。
and they eat about eight times as much tofu as americans do .	他們吃了八倍的美國人 。
more significant than what they eat is how they eat it .	更重要的是 , 牠們吃了什麼 。
they have all kinds of little strategies to keep from overeating , which , as you know , is a big problem here in america .	他們有各種各式各樣的策略 , 來避免你知道 , 這是美國最大的問題 。
a few of the strategies we observed: they eat off of smaller plates , so they tend to eat fewer calories at every sitting .	我們觀察其中的一些策略:他們吃少數的數量 , 所以它們通常會吃少數的能量 。
instead of serving family style , where you can sort of mindlessly eat as you're talking , they serve at the counter , put the food away , and then bring it to the table .	不是服務家店 , 把食物帶到桌上 , 然後把食物帶到桌上 。
they also have a 3 , 000yearold adage , which i think is the greatest sort of diet suggestion ever invented .	他們也有3 , 000歲的年齡 , 我認為這是最偉大的發明 。
it was invented by confucius .	它是由於混亂而發明 。
and that diet is known as the hara , hatchi , bu diet .	這種飲食被稱為 「 哈拉 」 、 「 哈拉 」 、 「 哈拉 」 、 「 漢堡 」 。
it's simply a little saying these people say before their meal to remind them to stop eating when their stomach is [80] percent full .	只是一個小小的說法 , 提醒他們不要吃飯 , 只剩下幾分之一的人說: 「 要提醒他們不要吃飯 。 」
it takes about a half hour for that full feeling to travel from your belly to your brain .	它花了大約半小時的時間 , 完全感受到你的大腦 。
and by remembering to stop at 80 percent it helps keep you from doing that very thing .	要記住 , 要停止80% , 可以幫助你做這件事 。
but , like sardinia , okinawa has a few social constructs that we can associate with longevity .	但 , 像薩丁尼亞 , 我們能與長壽的社會建構結合了一些社會建構 。
we know that isolation kills .	我們知道暴力殺害 。
fifteen years ago , the average american had three good friends .	五十年前 , 美國有三個好朋友 。
we're down to one and half right now .	我們現在就要到達一半 。
if you were lucky enough to be born in okinawa , you were born into a system where you automatically have a half a dozen friends with whom you travel through life .	如果你很幸運 , 生生在加州 , 你就生出生在水中 , 你出生在加州 , 你出生在五十多個朋友 , 你出生在你的人生中 。
they call it a moai . and if you're in a moai you're expected to share the bounty if you encounter luck , and if things go bad , child gets sick , parent dies , you always have somebody who has your back .	他們稱它為moai , 如果你在一個月球上 , 孩子會得到病患 , 生病 , 死亡 , 你永遠都有一些人 。
this particular moai , these five ladies have been together for 97 years .	這些五位女士都在97年開始 。
their average age is 102 .	他們的平均年齡是102 。
typically in america we've divided our adult life up into two sections .	通常在美國 , 我們把我們的成年分成兩半 。
there is our work life , where we're productive .	我們有工作生活 , 我們有生產力 。
and then one day , boom , we retire .	有一天 , 我們退休 。
and typically that has meant retiring to the easy chair , or going down to arizona to play golf .	基本上 , 它的意思是 , 要向高爾夫球隊去阿里桑達 。
in the okinawan language there is not even a word for retirement .	在尚未解放的詞語中 , 沒有一個字詞 。
instead there is one word that imbues your entire life , and that word is " ikigai . "	不論是 「 伊基加斯 」 的詞 , 這個詞是 「 伊基加斯 」 。
and , roughly translated , it means " the reason for which you wake up in the morning . "	翻譯 , 意思是: 「 你早上醒來的原因 。 」
for this 102yearold karate master , his ikigai was carrying forth this martial art .	在這102歲的凱特•馬斯特 , 他的kigai會帶著這位超棒的藝術 。
for this hundredyearold fisherman it was continuing to catch fish for his family three times a week .	在這百年的漁業 , 漁夫會持續捕捉漁夫 , 數百年來 , 漁夫會持續捕捉漁夫 。
and this is a question . the national institute on aging actually gave us a questionnaire to give these centenarians .	這是個問題 , 美國國會議員會提出一個問題 , 給予我們一個問題 。
and one of the questions , they were very culturally astute , the people who put the questionnaire .	其中一個問題之一是 , 他們是非常文化的 , 他們是非常文化的 , 他們是非常文化的 。
one of the questions was , " what is your ikigai ? "	其中一個問題是: 「 你的ikigai是什麼 ? 」
they instantly knew why they woke up in the morning .	他們很明顯知道為什麼他們在早上醒來 。
for this 102 year old woman , her ikigai was simply her greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	為了這個102歲的女性 , 她的三十二歲女子是她的孫女 。
two girls separated in age by 101 and a half years .	兩位女孩分離在101年半年 。
and i asked her what it felt like to hold a greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	我問她自己覺得什麼感覺像是抓住一個偉大的女兒 。
and she put her head back and she said , " it feels like leaping into heaven . "	她把她的頭帶回來 , 說: 「 感覺像是跳進天堂 。 」
i thought that was a wonderful thought .	我想那是很棒的思想 。
my editor at geographic wanted me to find america's blue zone .	我編輯的編輯要我找到美國的藍色區域 。
and for a while we looked on the prairies of minnesota , where actually there is a very high proportion of centenarians .	一旦我們看到了尼蘇達州的專家 , 那裡有非常高的比例 。
but that's because all the young people left .	但那是因為所有的年輕人 。
so , we turned to the data again .	所以 , 我們轉變了資料 。
and we found america's longestlived population among the seventhday adventists concentrated in and around loma linda , california .	我們發現美國最長壽的人口之一 , 在七天內 , 加州 , 加州 , 加州 。
adventists are conservative methodists .	傳統主義者是保守派的 。
they celebrate their sabbath from sunset on friday till sunset on saturday .	他們慶祝他們慶祝了星期六週日的日子 。
a " 24hour sanctuary in time , " they call it .	「 24小時聖經 」 , 他們稱之為 。
and they follow five little habits that conveys to them extraordinary longevity , comparatively speaking .	他們遵循了五個小習慣 , 讓他們很長壽 , 很長壽 。
in america here , life expectancy for the average woman is 80 .	在美國 , 平均女性有80% 。
but for an adventist woman , their life expectancy is 89 .	但 , 她們的人生期望是89歲 。
and the difference is even more pronounced among men , who are expected to live about 11 years longer than their american counterparts .	差異更廣告 , 比美國人數更高 , 他們預期壽命長達11年 。
now , this is a study that followed about 70 , 000 people for 30 years .	現在 , 這是一項研究 , 追蹤大約七萬人 。
sterling study . and i think it supremely illustrates the premise of this blue zone project .	史蒂夫 , 我覺得它很精確地說明了這個藍色區域的預期 。
this is a heterogeneous community .	這是個很大的社區 。
it's white , black , hispanic , asian .	它是白人、黑人、黑人、亞洲人 。
the only thing that they have in common are a set of very small lifestyle habits that they follow ritualistically for most of their lives .	他們唯一能做的是 , 他們所共享的習慣是一組非常小的生活習慣 , 讓他們遵循著最常見的習慣 。
they take their diet directly from the bible .	牠們會直接從聖經中挑選 。
genesis: chapter one , verse [29] , where god talks about legumes and seeds , and on one more stanza about green plants , ostensibly missing is meat .	基因:chpter , 上帝的演講 , 關於綠色植物 , 三分之二 , 不論是肉類 。
they take this sanctuary in time very serious .	他們把這條聖經的聖經當作非常嚴肅 。
for 24 hours every week , no matter how busy they are , how stressed out they are at work , where the kids need to be driven , they stop everything and they focus on their god , their social network , and then , hardwired right in the religion , are nature walks .	24小時 , 每個星期 , 不論他們有多忙碌 , 他們會停止一切 , 並且把他們放在上帝、社交網絡 , 然後 , 不論他們是多麼忙碌 , 他們就會停止一切 , 把一切放在上帝、社交網路 , 不論他們是多麼忙碌 。
and the power of this is not that it's done occasionally , the power is it's done every week for a lifetime .	權力是每週一生都沒有做過 。
none of it's hard . none of it costs money .	不需要錢 。
adventists also tend to hang out with other adventists .	傳統主義者也傾向於其他冒險主義者 。
so , if you go to an adventist's party you don't see people swilling jim beam or rolling a joint .	所以 , 如果你去一個專家的派對 , 你看不見有人穿著吉姆•貝姆或羅斯•福利 。
instead they're talking about their next nature walk , exchanging recipes , and yes , they pray .	相反地 , 他們會談到接下來的自然步行 , 是的 , 他們祈禱 。
but they influence each other in profound and measurable ways .	但它們對彼此影響彼此的影響 , 同時也影響彼此 。
this is a culture that has yielded ellsworth whareham .	這是一種文化 , 讓埃爾斯瓦哈姆 。
ellsworth whareham is 97 years old .	ellswham97歲 。
he's a multimillionaire , yet when a contractor wanted 6 , 000 dollars to build a privacy fence , he said , " for that kind of money i'll do it myself . "	他是多萬元 , 但當一個包容器想要6 , 000美元去建立一個隱私權利 , 他說: 「 為了那樣的錢來做我自己 。 」
so for the next three days he was out shoveling cement , and hauling poles around .	接下來的三天內 , 海克力克里斯逃跑 , 帶著走廊 。
and predictably , perhaps , on the fourth day he ended up in the operating room .	可能是 , 在第四天他終結到手術室 。
but not as the guy on the table ; the guy doing openheart surgery .	但不是在桌上 , 男子在桌上做開頭手術 。
at 97 he still does 20 openheart surgeries every month .	在97年 , 每個月都有20個開放的手術 。
ed rawlings , 103 years old now , an active cowboy , starts his morning with a swim .	老鼠 , 十三歲 , 一隻游泳 , 一隻游泳 。
and on weekends he likes to put on the boards , throw up rooster tails .	週末 , 他喜歡把它放進板塊上 , 丟下滑板 。
her grandson actually lives in the twin cities here .	她的祖先生在華盛頓市區 。
she starts her day with lifting weights .	她從那天開始 , 重量開始 。
she rides her bicycle .	她騎腳踏車 。
and then she gets in her rootbeer colored 1994 cadillac seville , and tears down the san bernardino freeway , where she still volunteers for seven different organizations .	接著 , 她在聖伯利斯•安德利的七個不同的組織中找到了七個不同的組織 。
i've been on 19 hardcore expeditions .	我已經在19個艱難的旅程中 。
i'm probably the only person you'll ever meet who rode his bicycle across the sahara desert without sunscreen .	我可能是唯一能遇見他在撒哈拉沙漠沒有陽光的人 。
but i'll tell you , there is no adventure more harrowing than riding shotgun with marge deton .	但我會告訴你們 , 沒有冒險的冒險 , 比起火星牛頓的爆炸還要多 。
" a stranger is a friend i haven't met yet ! " she'd say to me .	「 陌生人是我還沒見過的 , 她跟我說 。 」
so , what are the common denominators in these three cultures ?	所以 , 這些三種文化中的共同點是什麼 ?
what are the things that they all do ?	他們所做的一切是什麼 ?
and we managed to boil it down to nine .	然後我們管理了9.
in fact we've done two more blue zone expeditions since this and these common denominators hold true .	事實上 , 我們做了兩項藍色區塊 , 因為這和這些共同的調查 , 這些共同點的確保證 。
and the first one , and i'm about to utter a heresy here , none of them exercise , at least the way we think of exercise .	首先 , 我要把這段影片放在這裡 , 不管他們練習 , 至少我們思考運動的方式 。
instead , they set up their lives so that they are constantly nudged into physical activity .	相反地 , 牠們會不斷地進步到身體活動 。
these 100yearold okinawan women are getting up and down off the ground , they sit on the floor , 30 or 40 times a day .	這些百歲的女生在地面上下下 , 她們坐在地上 , 她們坐著樓上 , 三到四十歲 。
sardinians live in vertical houses , up and down the stairs .	sardiniansardinian住在垂直的房子 , 樓梯上 。
every trip to the store , or to church or to a friend's house occasions a walk .	每一趟旅程 , 或教堂或教堂或教堂 , 或去教堂 , 或去教堂 , 或去教堂 , 或去教堂 , 或去教堂 。
they don't have any conveniences .	他們沒有任何適應 。
there is not a button to push to do yard work or house work .	沒有一個按鈕 , 來推動 , 或家工作 。
if they want to mix up a cake , they're doing it by hand .	如果他們想要混合蛋糕 , 它們會用手做 。
that burns calories just as much as going on the treadmill does .	燃燒卡路里的卡路里就夠了 。
when they do do intentional physical activity , it's the things they enjoy . they tend to walk , the only proven way to stave off cognitive decline , and they all tend to have a garden .	當他們做獨立的活動時 , 唯一的進步就是要走路 , 僅僅僅僅是要走路 , 唯一能保證的進步 , 只能保持長期 。
they know how to set up their life in the right way so they have the right outlook .	他們知道如何把生命放在正確的情況下 , 讓他們有權利的權利 。
each of these cultures take time to downshift .	每個文化都有時間轉變 。
the sardinians pray . the seventhday adventists pray .	西班牙人的禱告 , 七天的祈禱 。
the okinawans have this ancestor veneration .	okinawan有這種祖先的靈感
but when you're in a hurry or stressed out , that triggers something called the inflammatory response , which is associated with everything from alzheimer's disease to cardiovascular disease .	但當你在傷害或壓力時 , 會觸發出一種叫做 「 炎反應 」 的反應 , 它與所有來自阿茲海默症有關的疾病有關 。
when you slow down for 15 minutes a day you turn that inflammatory state into a more antiinflammatory state .	當你慢慢十五分鐘 , 你就會轉變成更感染的狀態 。
they have vocabulary for sense of purpose , ikigai , like the okinawans .	他們有共同創作的特性 , 像是 「 阿薩瓦語 」 。
you know the two most dangerous years in your life are the year you're born , because of infant mortality , and the year you retire .	你知道在你人生中最危險的一年 , 你的生活中是一年 , 一年復活 。
these people know their sense of purpose , and they activate in their life , that's worth about seven years of extra life expectancy .	這些人知道他們的人生 , 值得7年的壽命 。
there's no longevity diet .	沒有長壽命 。
instead , these people drink a little bit every day , not a hard sell to the american population .	相反的 , 這些人每天都喝了一點點 , 不是賣給美國人口 。
they tend to eat a plantbased diet .	他們會吃植物的飲食 。
doesn't mean they don't eat meat , but lots of beans and nuts .	不代表他們不吃肉 , 但很多豆和牛肉 。
and they have strategies to keep from overeating , little things that nudge them away from the table at the right time .	他們有策略 , 讓它們從桌子上走出來 。
and then the foundation of all this is how they connect .	結果就是他們如何連結 。
they put their families first , take care of their children and their aging parents .	他們把他們的家人拿來 , 照顧他們的孩子和父母 。
they all tend to belong to a faithbased community , which is worth between four and 14 extra years of life expectancy if you do it four times a month .	他們都傾向於信仰基礎社群 , 每個月都要歸功於一千五十四次 。
and the biggest thing here is they also belong to the right tribe .	最重要的是 , 他們也屬於對部落 。
they were either born into or they proactively surrounded themselves with the right people .	他們是生長的 , 或他們把自己與對人的身分隔離 。
we know from the framingham studies , that if your three best friends are obese there is a 50 percent better chance that you'll be overweight .	我們知道 , 如果你的三個最好的朋友都觀察到 , 如果你三個最好的朋友 , 就會有更好的機會 。
so , if you hang out with unhealthy people , that's going to have a measurable impact over time .	所以 , 如果你與不健康的人 , 那將會有很大的影響力 。
instead , if your friend's idea of recreation is physical activity , bowling , or playing hockey , biking or gardening , if your friends drink a little , but not too much , and they eat right , and they're engaged , and they're trusting and trustworthy , that is going to have the biggest impact over time .	相反的 , 如果你的朋友喝了一點點 , 或花園 , 如果你的朋友喝了一點 , 但不太多 , 他們會受到影響 , 並且他們會對抗爭議 , 並且他們相信 , 和信任 , 會造成最大的影響 。
diets don't work . no diet in the history of the world has ever worked for more than two percent of the population .	沒有飲食 , 沒有飲食 , 全世界的人口數量超過百分之二 。
exercise programs usually start in january ; they're usually done by october .	練習通常會開始在日本中 , 通常是一月 。
when it comes to longevity there is no short term fix in a pill or anything else .	直到長壽 , 沒有短暫的詞彙 , 或其他東西 。
but when you think about it , your friends are longterm adventures , and therefore , perhaps the most significant thing you can do to add more years to your life , and life to your years . thank you very much .	但當你思考一下 , 你的朋友長期冒險 , 可能是最重要的事情 , 你能花更多年的時間才能做到 。 謝謝大家 。
ink that conducts electricity ; a window that turns from clear to opaque at the flip of a switch ; a jelly that makes music . all this stuff exists , and catarina mota says: it's time to play with it . mota leads us on a tour of surprising and cool new materials , and suggests that the way we'll figure out what they're good for is to experiment , tinker and have fun .	用這種東西來做 , 和酷的新材料 , 讓音樂出現了 。 所有這些東西都存在 , 卡塔里娜莫塔里娜莫特說: 「 時間玩樂 , 讓音樂有趣 。 」 和酷的新材料 , 我們會發現 , 讓音樂有趣 , 和酷的新材料 , 我們會想出什麼 , 讓音樂有趣 。
creativity , design , technology	創造力、設計、科技 。
catarina mota: play with smart materials	catarinamota:玩耍聰明的材料 。
i have a friend in portugal whose grandfather built a vehicle out of a bicycle and a washing machine so he could transport his family .	我有一位朋友 , 一間飛行器 , 他可以運送他的家人 。
he did it because he couldn't afford a car , but also because he knew how to build one .	他這麼做 , 因為他知道如何建造一個 。
there was a time when we understood how things worked and how they were made , so we could build and repair them , or at the very least make informed decisions about what to buy .	有時候 , 我們了解如何運作和如何運作 , 我們了解它們如何運作 , 以及它們如何運作 , 所以我們可以建造、修復它們 , 或至少在做些什麼是如何做的事 。
many of these doityourself practices were lost in the second half of the 20th century .	在20世紀中 , 許多人工程師都失敗了 。
but now , the maker community and the opensource model are bringing this kind of knowledge about how things work and what they're made of back into our lives , and i believe we need to take them to the next level , to the components things are made of .	但現在 , 製造家社區和開放原始碼的模型就是把它們帶到下一個層面 , 讓大家知道它們是如何運作的 , 以及我們的生活中 , 我相信我們需要把它們帶到下一個階層 , 讓它們變成我們的生活 。
for the most part , we still know what traditional materials like paper and textiles are made of and how they are produced .	大部分的部份 , 我們仍然知道傳統材料像是紙、紡織品 , 以及它們如何生產 。
but now we have these amazing , futuristic composites plastics that change shape , paints that conduct electricity , pigments that change color , fabrics that light up .	但現在我們有了這些令人驚奇的生物 , 塑膠會改變顏色 , 製造電力 , 製造電力 , 製造出電力 , 製造出電力 , 那些改變顏色的塑膠 。
let me show you some examples .	讓我給你們一些例子 。
so conductive ink allows us to paint circuits instead of using the traditional printed circuit boards or wires .	使用傳統印刷電路板或線線 , 可以用傳統印刷電路板或線線 。
in the case of this little example i'm holding , we used it to create a touch sensor that reacts to my skin by turning on this little light .	在這個小小的例子中 , 我們用它來創造一個觸碰感應器 , 用它來創造一個觸碰感應器 , 用它來創造一個觸碰感應器 。
conductive ink has been used by artists , but recent developments indicate that we will soon be able to use it in laser printers and pens .	工藝品被藝術家設計出來 , 但最近的發展顯示 , 我們很快就能夠用它在雷射印刷機和鉛筆 。
and this is a sheet of acrylic infused with colorless lightdiffusing particles .	這是一顆原始的微粒子 , 加強了無色無色的光譜 。
what this means is that , while regular acrylic only diffuses light around the edges , this one illuminates across the entire surface when i turn on the lights around it .	意思是 , 當光線穿越整個表面時 , 我會把燈光放在邊緣 。
two of the known applications for this material include interior design and multitouch systems .	這種材料包含了二種知識應用程式 , 包括設計和多觸控系統 。
and thermochromic pigments change color at a given temperature .	氣候變色的顏色會改變顏色 。
so i'm going to place this on a hot plate that is set to a temperature only slightly higher than ambient and you can see what happens .	所以我要把這個放在一個熱板上 , 讓一個溫度非常高 , 比你所能看到的還要高 。
so one of the principle applications for this material is , amongst other things , in baby bottles , so it indicates when the contents are cool enough to drink .	這種材料的原則之一是 , 在寶寶瓶裡 , 很酷足的 , 可以喝酒 。
so these are just a few of what are commonly known as smart materials .	這些只是一些常常被稱為聰明的材料 。
in a few years , they will be in many of the objects and technologies we use on a daily basis .	幾年內 , 它們會在許多我們使用的物體和技術上使用 。
we may not yet have the flying cars science fiction promised us , but we can have walls that change color depending on temperature , keyboards that roll up , and windows that become opaque at the flick of a switch .	我們可能還沒有飛行車庫 , 但我們可以有牆壁 , 改變顏色的牆壁 , 改變顏色 , 轉換顏色 , 轉換顏色 , 轉換顏色 , 轉換顏色 , 轉換顏色 , 轉換成果蠅 。
so i'm a social scientist by training , so why am i here today talking about smart materials ?	所以 , 為什麼我今天要談的是智慧型材料 ?
well first of all , because i am a maker .	首先 , 因為我是個製造者 。
i'm curious about how things work and how they are made , but also because i believe we should have a deeper understanding of the components that make up our world , and right now , we don't know enough about these hightech composites our future will be made of .	我很好奇他們是如何運作的 , 但也是因為我相信我們應該更深入了解它們如何運作 , 和它們如何運作 , 但也是因為我相信我們應該更深入了解我們的未來會如何運作 。
smart materials are hard to obtain in small quantities .	聰明的材料很難在小量子中找到 。
there's barely any information available on how to use them , and very little is said about how they are produced .	幾乎沒有任何資訊可以運用它們 , 很少是說他們如何生產 。
so for now , they exist mostly in this realm of trade secrets and patents only universities and corporations have access to .	所以 , 現在 , 大部分都存在於貿易秘密和專利 , 只有大學和企業都能取得 。
so a little over three years ago , kirsty boyle and i started a project we called open materials .	三年前 , 我開始了一個計畫叫做開放材料 。
it's a website where we , and anyone else who wants to join us , share experiments , publish information , encourage others to contribute whenever they can , and aggregate resources such as research papers and tutorials by other makers like ourselves .	它是個網站 , 我們和任何人想要加入我們 , 分享實驗 , 分享實驗 , 發表資訊 , 鼓勵其他人想要加入我們 , 分享實驗 , 發布資訊 , 鼓勵其他人想要加入我們 , 分享實驗 , 發布資訊 , 鼓勵其他人想要加入我們 , 分享實驗 , 發布資訊 , 鼓勵其他人想要加入我們 , 分享實驗 , 發布資訊 , 鼓勵其他人想要加入我們 。
we would like it to become a large , collectively generated database of doityourself information on smart materials .	我們會喜歡它成為一個大型的資料庫 , 集體化合物的資料庫 。
but why should we care how smart materials work and what they are made of ?	但為什麼我們要關心智慧型材料的工作 , 以及他們所做的事 ?
first of all , because we can't shape what we don't understand , and what we don't understand and use ends up shaping us .	首先 , 因為我們無法形容我們不了解的事物 , 以及我們不了解的事物 , 以及我們不了解的事物 。
the objects we use , the clothes we wear , the houses we live in , all have a profound impact on our behavior , health and quality of life .	我們使用的物品 , 衣服 , 衣服 , 衣服 , 衣服我們生活在我們的行為、健康和生活品質上 。
so if we are to live in a world made of smart materials , we should know and understand them .	所以 , 如果我們要活在一個充滿智慧型的材料 , 我們應該知道 , 了解它們 。
secondly , and just as important , innovation has always been fueled by tinkerers .	第二 , 創新 , 一直都被推動了 。
so many times , amateurs , not experts , have been the inventors and improvers of things ranging from mountain bikes to semiconductors , personal computers , airplanes .	許多時候 , 演員、個人電腦、飛機 , 都沒有專家 。
the biggest challenge is that material science is complex and requires expensive equipment .	最大的挑戰是 , 材料科學是複雜且需要昂貴的設備 。
but that's not always the case .	但這並不總是如此 。
two scientists at university of illinois understood this when they published a paper on a simpler method for making conductive ink .	兩位科學家 , 在伊利諾州大學的研究發現 , 當他們出版了一張紙 , 用簡單的方法來製造出版本 。
jordan bunker , who had had no experience with chemistry until then , read this paper and reproduced the experiment at his maker space using only offtheshelf substances and tools .	jordanbunker , 他沒有經歷過化學 , 直到那之後 , 閱讀這篇文章 , 讓他做實驗的實驗 , 透過化學 , 直到那之後 , 閱讀這篇文章 , 用它來做實驗 。
he used a toaster oven , and he even made his own vortex mixer , based on a tutorial by another scientist/maker .	他用了一連串的曲線 , 以另一位科學家/maker , 為他創造出自己的創作 。
jordan then published his results online , including all the things he had tried and didn't work , so others could study and reproduce it .	jordan在網上搜尋了他的結果 , 包括所有他嘗試的結果 , 沒有工作 , 所以其他人可以研究並繁殖它 。
so jordan's main form of innovation was to take an experiment created in a wellequipped lab at the university and recreate it in a garage in chicago using only cheap materials and tools he made himself .	jordan主要的創作就是把一個實驗創造出一個實驗 , 在芝加哥使用唯一便宜的材料和工具 , 讓他自己做 。
and now that he published this work , others can pick up where he left and devise even simpler processes and improvements .	現在 , 他出版了這項工作 , 其他人可以選擇離開 , 更容易處理和改善 。
another example i'd like to mention her project's goal is to highlight the expressive qualities of materials while focusing on the creativity and skills of the builder .	另外一個例子 , 我想要提倡她專案計畫的目標是要提高專注在創造力和技能上創造力和技能 。
electronics kits are very powerful in that they teach us how things work , but the constraints inherent in their design influence the way we learn .	電子裝置是非常強大的 , 他們教導我們學習如何運作 , 但在他們教導我們學習如何運作時 , 電子裝置非常強大 。
so hannah's approach , on the other hand , is to formulate a series of techniques for creating unusual objects that free us from predesigned constraints by teaching us about the materials themselves .	漢娜 , 另一方面 , 用了一系列的技巧 , 來創造出一種不尋常的物品 , 來創造出我們不尋常的物品 , 來創造出不尋常的物品 , 來創造出我們不尋常的物品 , 來創造出不尋常的物品 , 來創造出我們不尋常的物品 。

but i had no idea that car was stopping , and i think we can do a lot better than that .	但我不知道汽車停止了 , 我認為我們能做得更好 。

in the future , with cars exchanging data with each other , we will be able to see not just three cars ahead and three cars behind , to the right and left , all at the same time , bird's eye view , we will actually be able to see into those cars .	在未來 , 我們將能看到這些車輛 , 不只有三輛車輛 , 和左邊 , 同時 , 我們會看到這些車輛 , 和左邊 , 同時 , 我們會看到這些車輛 。

and with computation and algorithms and predictive models , we will be able to see the future .	通過計算、演算法和預測模型 , 我們將會看到未來 。

cars are threedimensional objects that have a fixed position and velocity .	汽車是三維空間的物體 , 它有固定的位置和速度 。
they travel down roads .	他們走路 。
often they travel on prepublished routes .	通常他們會旅行在前出版的路線 。
it's really not that hard to make reasonable predictions about where a car's going to be in the near future .	真的不難以預測汽車未來的預測 。
even if , when you're in your car and some motorcyclist comes bshoom ! 85 miles an hour down , lanesplitting i know you've had this experience that guy didn't " just come out of nowhere . "	即使 , 當你在車子裡 , 摩托車和摩托車司機 , 一小時下 , 八十五英哩時 , 我知道你有這樣的經驗 , 沒有 「 只是走出去了 。 」

i mean , they're newtonian objects .	我的意思是 , 他們是牛頓的物體 。
that's very nice about them .	對他們來說很棒 。
so how do we get there ?	所以我們要怎麼做到呢 ?
we can start with something as simple as sharing our position data between cars , just sharing gps .	我們可以從簡單的角度來看 , 分享gps 。
if i have a gps and a camera in my car , i have a pretty precise idea of where i am and how fast i'm going .	如果我有一台攝影機在我的車裡 , 我有很精準的點子 , 我有很精準的點子 , 我有很精準的點子 , 我有很精準的點子 , 我有很精準的點子 ,
with computer vision , i can estimate where the cars around me are , sort of , and where they're going .	透過電腦視覺 , 我可以估計我在哪裡移動的車 , 以及他們在哪裡 。

professor bob wang and his team have done computer simulations of what happens when fuzzy estimates combine , even in light traffic , when cars just share gps data , and we've moved this research out of the computer simulation and into robot test beds that have the actual sensors that are in cars now on these robots: stereo cameras , gps , and the twodimensional laser range finders that are common in backup systems .	教授和他的團隊完成了電腦模擬器 , 當車輛分享gps , 我們已經把這項研究應用在電腦模擬器上 , 當車輛分享gps , 我們已經把這個研究應用在電腦模擬器上 , 和他的團隊完成了電腦模擬器 , 當汽車分享gps時 , 我們已經把這個電腦模擬出來 , 和他的團隊完成了電腦模擬器 , 我們已經把這個研究應用在電腦模擬裝置上 , 和他的團隊完成了電腦模擬器 , 我們已經把這個研究應用在電腦模擬器上 。
we also attach a discrete shortrange communication radio , and the robots talk to each other .	我們也把音頻傳播頻率傳播 , 機器人彼此互相溝通 。
when these robots come at each other , they track each other's position precisely , and they can avoid each other .	當這些機器人互相互相作用時 , 它們會追蹤彼此的位置 , 牠們可以避免彼此 。
we're now adding more and more robots into the mix , and we encountered some problems .	現在 , 我們加入了一些問題 , 越來越多的機器人進入混合物中 , 我們會遇到一些問題 。
one of the problems , when you get too much chatter , it's hard to process all the packets , so you have to prioritize , and that's where the predictive model helps you .	其中一個問題是 , 當你太多聊天時 , 要處理所有包包 , 你得先做最佳的模式幫助你 。
if your robot cars are all tracking the predicted trajectories , you don't pay as much attention to those packets .	如果你的機器人汽車是追蹤預測軌跡 , 你不會注意到這些包包 。
you prioritize the one guy who seems to be going a little off course .	你把一個傢伙看起來很小 。
that guy could be a problem .	這傢伙可能是個問題 。
and you can predict the new trajectory .	你可以預測新軌跡 。
so you don't only know that he's going off course , you know how .	所以你不只知道他會怎麼做 。
and you know which drivers you need to alert to get out of the way .	你知道 , 駕駛你需要放棄路徑 。
and we wanted to do how can we best alert everyone ?	我們想要做我們最好的目標嗎 ?
how can these cars whisper , " you need to get out of the way ? "	這些車如何: 「 你需要從哪裡來 ? 」
well , it depends on two things: one , the ability of the car , and second the ability of the driver .	嗯 , 它依賴兩件事:一、汽車的能力 , 以及第二個駕駛的能力 。
if one guy has a really great car , but they're on their phone or , you know , doing something , they're not probably in the best position to react in an emergency .	如果一個人有一個很棒的車 , 但他們在電話 , 或你知道 , 做一些事 , 他們並不可能在最好的位置上做些什麼 。
so we started a separate line of research doing driver state modeling .	所以我們開始了一系列的研究執行模式 。
and now , using a series of three cameras , we can detect if a driver is looking forward , looking away , looking down , on the phone , or having a cup of coffee .	現在 , 使用一系列三台攝影機 , 我們可以偵測到駕駛 , 或喝杯咖啡 。
we can predict the accident and we can predict who , which cars , are in the best position to move out of the way to calculate the safest route for everyone .	我們可以預測 , 我們能預測 , 在最好的情況下 , 可以預測 , 誰 , 車子是最好的位置 , 讓每個人都能在最好的位置 。
fundamentally , these technologies exist today .	基本上 , 這些技術存在今天 。
i think the biggest problem that we face is our own willingness to share our data .	我認為最大的問題是 , 我們面對的是我們自己願意分享我們的資料 。
i think it's a very disconcerting notion , this idea that our cars will be watching us , talking about us to other cars , that we'll be going down the road in a sea of gossip .	我認為這是一個非常令人沮喪的概念 , 我們的車子會在海裡看到我們 , 和其他車輛走路 , 我們會在海上看到我們 。
but i believe it can be done in a way that protects our privacy , just like right now , when i look at your car from the outside , i don't really know about you .	但我相信它可以做得以保護我們的隱私 , 就像現在 , 當我看著你的車從外面看 , 我並不知道你 。
if i look at your license plate number , i don't really know who you are .	如果我仔細看你的數字 , 我並不知道你是誰 。
i believe our cars can talk about us behind our backs .	我相信汽車可以在我們的背後說我們 。
and i think it's going to be a great thing .	我認為這將會是個很棒的事 。
i want you to consider for a moment if you really don't want the distracted teenager behind you to know that you're braking , that you're coming to a dead stop .	我想請各位想像一下 , 如果你真的不希望你有一刻 , 要你知道你是勇敢的 , 你就會死去 。
by sharing our data willingly , we can do what's best for everyone .	透過分享我們的資料 , 我們就能為每個人做最好的事 。
so let your car gossip about you .	咱們來談一下你 。
it's going to make the roads a lot safer .	它會讓道路更安全 。

business , flight , science , short talk , space , technology , universe	商業、科學、短談、空間、科技、宇宙 。
peter diamandis on stephen hawking in zero g	史蒂芬•霍金在西班牙 。
those of you who know me know how passionate i am about opening the space frontier .	你們知道我知道我的熱情是如何開放空間的 。
so when i had the chance to give the world's expert in gravity the experience of zero gravity , it was incredible .	所以當我有機會給世界專家 , 它很奇妙 。
and i want to tell you that story .	我想告訴各位的故事 。

becky blanton planned to live in her van for a year and see the country , but when depression set in and her freelance job ended , her camping trip turned into homelessness . in this intimate talk , she describes her experience of becoming one of america's working homeless .	貝琪•布蘭頓計劃到家鄉 , 但當憂鬱和她隔離了一年後 , 看到國家 , 但當憂鬱症和她所經歷的經歷成為美國人工作時 , 她的經歷變得無家可歸 。
adventure , happiness , life , personal growth , poverty , social change , society , storytelling	冒險、幸福、生活、社會、社會、改變、社會、社會、社會、改變、社會、社會、改變、社群、社會、改變、社群 。
becky blanton: the year i was homeless	貝琪.布蘭頓:一年我無家可歸 。
i'm a writer and a journalist , and i'm also an insanely curious person , so in 22 years as a journalist , i've learned how to do a lot of new things .	我是個作家和記者 , 我已經學到了很多新的事物 。
and three years ago , one of the things i learned how to do was to become invisible .	三年前 , 我學到了一件事情 , 就是要成為隱形 。
i became one of the working homeless .	我成為了一家無家可歸的人 。
i quit my job as a newspaper editor after my father died in february of that same year , and decided to travel .	我辭職 , 決定去旅行 , 決定去旅行 。
his death hit me pretty hard .	他的死亡非常困難 。
and there were a lot of things that i wanted to feel and deal with while i was doing that .	有許多東西 , 我想要感覺和處理我在做的事 。
i've camped my whole life . and i decided that living in a van for a year to do this would be like one long camping trip .	我花了一整年的時間去做這段旅程 。 我決定住在一個旅行的旅程中 。
so i packed my cat , my rottweiler and my camping gear into a 1975 chevy van , and drove off into the sunset , having fully failed to realize three critical things .	於是我帶著我的貓 , 開車開車 , 開車到1975年的開車 , 開車開車 , 全部都失敗了 , 完成了三件關鍵的事情 。
one: that society equates living in a permanent structure , even a shack , with having value as a person .	第一:社會平均生活在永久的結構中 , 甚至是一群人 , 甚至是一個人 。
two: i failed to realize how quickly the negative perceptions of other people can impact our reality , if we let it .	第二:我失敗了 , 大家可以影響我們的現實 , 如果我們讓他人能影響我們的現實 。
three: i failed to realize that homelessness is an attitude , not a lifestyle .	第三:我失敗 , 意識到無家可歸是一種態度 , 而不是生活方式 。
at first , living in the van was great .	首先 , 生活在空中很棒 。
i showered in campgrounds . i ate out regularly .	我在校園裡演出 , 我經常在營地 。
and i had time to relax and to grieve .	我有時間放鬆和悲傷 。
but then the anger and the depression about my father's death set in .	但 , 憤怒和憂鬱 , 我父親的死亡 。
my freelance job ended . and i had to get a fulltime job to pay the bills .	我的自由工作結束了 , 我必須得到一整份工作 。
what had been a really mild spring turned into a miserably hot summer .	一個非常熱的夏天 , 一個非常熱的夏天 。
and it became impossible to park anywhere without being very obvious that i had a cat and a dog with me , and it was really hot .	沒有很明顯的 , 我有一隻貓和一隻貓狗 , 我有一隻貓和一隻貓狗 , 我有一隻貓和一隻狗 , 很明顯 。
the cat came and went through an open window in the van .	凱特走過一間開放窗戶 。
the doggy went into doggy day care .	狗花了幾天 。
whenever i could , i used employee showers in office buildings and truck stops .	只要我可以 , 我用員工在辦公室大樓和卡車停下來 。
or i washed up in public rest rooms .	或我在公共場合的房間裡 。
nighttime temperatures in the van rarely dropped below 80 degrees fahrenheit , making it difficult or impossible to sleep .	夜晚的溫度降低80度的溫度 , 無法睡眠 。
food rotted in the heat .	食物在熱裡的食物 。
ice in my ice chest melted within hours , and it was pretty miserable .	我冰河在幾小時內的冰河流行 , 它很可怕 。
i couldn't afford to find an apartment , or couldn't afford an apartment that would allow me to have the rottweiler and the cat .	我無法負擔得起一個公寓 , 或不能負擔得起一個公寓 , 或無法負擔得起的公寓 , 或不能負擔得起公寓 。
and i refused to give them up , so i stayed in the van .	我拒絕給他們放棄 , 所以我留在那裡 。
and when the heat made me too sick to walk the 50 feet to the public restroom outside my van at night , i used a bucket and a trash bag as a toilet .	當熱情讓我太生氣時 , 我用一塊垃圾袋和垃圾袋 。
when winter weather set in , the temperatures dropped below freezing . and they stayed there .	當冬天天氣融合時 , 溫度降低了 , 溫度降低了 , 溫度降低了 。
and i faced a whole new set of challenges .	我面對了一個全新的挑戰 。
i parked a different place every night so i would avoid being noticed and hassled by the police .	我每天晚上停下來 , 我會避免注意到 , 被警察打開 。
i didn't always succeed .	我不總是成功 。
but i felt out of control of my life .	但我感覺到我的人生 。
and i don't know when or how it happened , but the speed at which i went from being a talented writer and journalist to being a homeless woman , living in a van , took my breath away .	我不知道何時發生什麼事 , 但是我從一名作家和記者身上學到的 , 是我從一個很有名的作家和記者 , 來到一個無家可歸的女人 , 生活在一個無家可歸的家裡 , 讓我呼吸 。
i hadn't changed . my i . q . hadn't dropped .	我沒有改變 , 我沒有改變 。 我的智商 , 沒有改變 。
my talent , my integrity , my values , everything about me remained the same .	我的確信、我的價值、我的價值 , 每件事都一樣 。
but i had changed somehow .	但我已經改變了 。
i spiraled deeper and deeper into a depression .	我深深深入憂鬱 。
and eventually someone referred me to a homeless health clinic .	最後有人把我帶到一個無家的醫療診所 。
and i went . i hadn't bathed in three days .	我在三天內完成了 。
i was as smelly and as depressed as anyone in line .	我很像任何人一樣 , 身為任何人 。
i just wasn't drunk or high .	我只是不喝或高興 。
and when several of the homeless men realized that , including a former university professor , they said , " you aren't homeless . why are you really here ? "	當幾位沒有家人意識到 , 包括一位前大學教授 , 他們說: 「 你不是家人 。 為什麼你在這裡 ? 」
other homeless people didn't see me as homeless , but i did .	其他無家可歸的家人都看過我 , 但是我做了 。
then the professor listened to my story and he said , " you have a job . you have hope .	教授聽我的故事 , 他說: 「 你有個工作 , 你有希望 。
the real homeless don't have hope . "	真正的家人沒有希望 。 」
a reaction to the medication the clinic gave me for my depression left me suicidal . and i remember thinking , " if i killed myself , no one would notice . "	診所給了我的憂鬱症 , 我記得我在想: 「 如果我殺了我自己 , 沒有人會注意 。 」
a friend told me , shortly after that , that she had heard that tim russert , a nationally renowned journalist , had been talking about me on national t . v .	一個朋友告訴我 , 很久後 , 她聽說過 , 一個全國的記者 , 她聽說過 , 一個全國的記者 , 一直在談論我 。
an essay i'd written about my father , the year before he died , was in tim's new book .	我寫了一篇關於我父親的故事 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死前 , 在他死
and he was doing the talk show circuit . and he was talking about my writing .	他在講我的寫作 , 他在談論我的寫作 。
and when i realized that tim russert , former moderator of " meet the press , " was talking about my writing , while i was living in a van in a walmart parking lot , i started laughing .	當我意識到 , 「 公園 」 時 , 我開始笑聲 。
i started laughing because it got to the point where , was i a writer , or was i a homeless woman ?	我開始笑 , 因為它到哪裡 , 我是作家 , 還是我是一位作家呢 ?
so i went in the bookstore . and i found tim's book .	所以我去了書 , 我發現了tim的書 。
and i stood there . and i reread my essay .	我站在那裡 , 我把我丟掉了 。
because i was a writer .	因為我是作家 。
i was a writer .	我是作家 。
shortly after that i moved back to tennessee .	短暫之後 , 我搬到海岸 。
i alternated between living in a van and couch surfing with friends .	我住在一個飯店與朋友之間 , 與朋友交談 。
and i started writing again .	我開始寫作 。
by the summer of the following year i was a working journalist .	今年夏天 , 我是一位記者 。
i was winning awards . i was living in my own apartment .	我是贏得獎勵 , 我在我自己的公寓 。
i was no longer homeless .	我不再無家可歸 。
and i was no longer invisible .	我不再看不見 。
thousands of people work full and parttime jobs , and live in their cars .	數以千計的人工作 , 生活在汽車上 。
but society continues to stigmatize and criminalize living in your vehicle or on the streets .	但社會持續著嚴格 , 或街道上的街道 。
so the homeless , the working homeless , primarily remain invisible .	所以 , 無家可歸 , 無家可歸 , 無家可歸 。
but if you ever meet one , engage them , encourage them , and offer them hope .	但如果你遇見過一個人 , 他們鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 , 鼓勵他們 ,
the human spirit can overcome anything if it has hope .	人類的精神可以克服任何東西 , 如果它有希望 。
and i'm not here to be the poster girl for the homeless .	我不是在這裡 , 要成為一位在家鄉的女生 。
i'm not here to encourage you to give money to the next panhandler you meet .	我不是要鼓勵你去到下一個巴勒斯坦堡 。
but i am here to tell you that , based on my experience , people are not where they live , where they sleep , or what their life situation is at any given time .	但我在這裡要告訴各位 , 基於我的經驗 , 人們並不是住在他們生活中 , 或他們生活在哪裡 。
three years ago i was living in a van in a walmart parking lot , and today i'm speaking at ted .	三年前 , 我在華盛頓特區公園 , 今天我正在ted演講 。
hope always , always finds a way . thank you .	希望總是找到方法 。 謝謝 。
at tedxchange , thailand's " mr . condom , " mechai viravaidya , walks us through the country's bold plan to raise its standard of living , starting in the 1970s . first step: population control . and that means a lot of frank , funny and very effective talk about condoms .	tedxchangethailand是 「 mr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、 「 domr 」 、
culture , global issues , health , population , science	文化、全球議題、健康、人口、科學 。
mechai viravaidya: how mr . condom made thailand a better place	伊維拉瓦達:mr , 會議會讓泰國更好 。
now , when i was a young man 40 years ago , the country was very , very poor with lots and lots and lots of people living in poverty .	當時我年輕人四十年前 , 國家非常貧窮 , 許多人生活在貧困中 。
we decided to do something about it , but we didn't begin with a welfare program or a poverty reduction program .	我們決定要做點什麼 , 但我們沒有開始用一個公平的計畫 , 或貧窮的計畫 。
but we began with a familyplanning program , following a very successful maternal child health activity , sets of activities .	但我們從一個家庭計畫開始 , 追蹤一個非常成功的兒童健康活動 。
so basically , no one would accept family planning if their children didn't survive .	基本上 , 沒有人會接受家庭計劃如果孩子沒有生存 。
so the first step: get to the children , get to the mothers , and then follow up with family planning .	第一個步驟:給孩子們 , 和家庭計劃有關 。
not just child mortality alone , you need also family planning .	不僅僅是孩子的死亡率 , 你也需要家庭計畫 。
now let me take you back as to why we needed to do it .	現在讓我帶各位回到我們需要做的事 。
in my country , that was the case in 1974 .	在我的國家 , 那是1974年 。
seven children per family tremendous growth at 3 . 3 percent .	7個孩子 , 每家有7個孩子 , 成長3.3% 。
there was just no future .	沒有未來 。
we needed to reduce the population growth rate .	我們需要減少人口成長率 。
so we said , " let's do it . "	所以我們說: 「 咱們來做 。 」
the women said , " we agree . we'll use pills , but we need a doctor to prescribe the pills , " and we had very , very few doctors .	婦女說: 「 我們同意 , 但我們需要一個醫生 , 來治療我們的藥品 , 但我們需要一個醫生 。 」
we didn't take no as an answer ; we took no as a question .	我們沒辦法解決問題 。
we went to the nurses and the midwives , who were also women , and did a fantastic job at explaining how to use the pill .	我們去了護士和同性戀者 , 她們也是女性 , 做了一個很棒的工作 , 來解釋如何使用藥品 。
that was wonderful , but it covered only 20 percent of the country .	這很棒 , 但它只佔了20%的國家 。
what do we do for the other 80 percent leave them alone and say , " well , they're not medical personnel . "	另外80%的人會說: 「 嗯 , 他們不是醫療人 。 」
no , we decided to do a bit more .	不 , 我們決定要做更多 。
so we went to the ordinary people that you saw .	所以 , 我們去了你看到的一般人 。
actually , below that yellow sign i wish they hadn't wiped that , because there was " cocacola " there .	其實 , 我希望他們還沒拿到這個黃色標誌 , 因為有 「 卡科拉 」 。
we were so much bigger than cocacola in those days .	我們比卡卡多得多大 。
and no difference , the people they chose were the people we chose .	沒有差異 , 他們選擇的人民就是我們選擇的 。
they were wellknown in the community , they knew that customers were always right , and they were terrific , and they practiced their family planning themselves .	在社區中 , 他們知道客戶是很棒的 , 他們知道客戶總是是對的 , 而且他們很恐怖 , 而且他們很恐怖 , 他們也很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們很害怕 , 他們也很害怕 , 他們
so they could supply pills and condoms throughout the country , in every village of the country .	所以他們可以供應所有村莊 , 全國各地的村落 。
so there we are . we went to the people who were seen as the cause of the problem to be the solution .	所以 , 我們去了那些被視為解決方案的人 。
wherever there were people and you can see boats with the women , selling things here's the floating market selling bananas and crabs and also contraceptives wherever you find people , you'll find contraceptives in thailand .	在那裡 , 你會找到人 , 賣香蕉、螃蟹 , 還有交易 , 賣香蕉、販賣香蕉、販賣香蕉、賣香蕉、賣香蕉、賣香蕉、賣香蕉、賣香蕉、賣香蕉、商品 。
and then we decided , why not get to religion because in the philippines , the catholic church was pretty strong , and thai people were buddhist .	接著 , 我們決定 , 不是因為在菲律教堂 , 教堂很強大 , 教堂很強大 , 教堂很強大 , 教堂也很強壯 。
we went to them and they said , " look , could you help us ? "	我們去找他們 , 說: 「 看 , 你能幫我們嗎 ? 」
i'm there the one in blue , not the yellow holding a bowl of holy water for the monk to sprinkle holy water on pills and condoms for the sanctity of the family .	我是藍色的 , 不是黃色的 , 黃色會帶著一碗水 , 帶著一碗水 , 帶著一碗水 , 帶著一碗水 , 讓家人吃飯 。
and this picture was sent throughout the country .	這張照片是來自國家的 。
so some of the monks in the villages were doing the same thing themselves .	村莊裡的一些猴子都做同樣的事 。
and the women were saying , " no wonder we have no sideeffects .	女人會說: 「 不想我們沒有對方 。
it's been blessed . "	很幸福 。 」
that was their perception .	那就是他們的感知 。
and then we went to teachers .	然後我們去教導 。
you need everybody to be involved in trying to provide whatever it is that make humanity a better place .	你需要每個人都參與嘗試提供任何東西 , 讓人類更好的地方 。
so we went to the teachers .	所以我們去了老師 。
over a quarter of a million were taught about family planning with a new alphabet a , b for birth , c for condom , i for iud , v for vasectomy .	超過四分之三十五萬人都被教導關於家庭計畫 , 用新字母 , 來源頭 , 以新字母 , 為生存 , 為了保育 , 為了保證 , 我會用新字母來做 , 為我所知 。
and then we had a snakes and ladders game , where you throw dice .	接著 , 我們有蛇和拉登遊戲 , 你會丟掉 。
if you land on anything profamily planning , you move ahead .	如果你在任何公平的規劃中 , 你就會移動 。
like , " mother takes the pill every night .	比如: 「 媽媽每天晚上吃午餐 。
very good , mother . move ahead .	非常好 , 媽媽 。
uncle buys a condom . very good , uncle . move ahead .	叔叔很好 , 叔叔 , 非常好 , 叔叔 。
uncle gets drunk , doesn't use condom . come back , start again . "	叔叔很快 , 沒用它 , 再次回來 。 」
again , education , class entertainment .	再一次 , 教育 , 娛樂 。
and the kids were doing it in school too .	孩子們也在學校 。
we had relay races with condoms , we had children's condomblowing championship .	我們有孩子的共享 , 和保守派 , 我們有孩子的自主權 。
and before long , the condom was know as the girl's best friend .	不久之後 , 保證會成為女孩最好的朋友 。
in thailand , for poor people , diamonds don't make it so the condom is the girl's best friend .	在thailand , 窮人 , 鑽石不會製造它 , 是因為女孩最好的朋友 。
we introduced our first microcredit program in 1975 , and the women who organized it said , " we only want to lend to women who practice family planning .	我們在1975年發佈了第一位微軟的工程師 , 她說: 「 我們只想讓女性接受家庭規劃 。
if you're pregnant , take care of your pregnancy .	如果你懷孕 , 保持懷孕 。
if you're not pregnant , you can take a loan out from us . "	如果你不懷孕 , 你就能帶領貸款 。 」
and that was run by them .	結果是他們 。
and after 35/36 years , it's still going on .	在36年後 , 仍然會發生 。
it's a part of the village development bank ; it's not a real bank , but it's a fund microcredit .	這是村莊發展銀行的一部分 , 但它是一項基金 。
and we didn't need a big organization to run it it was run by the villagers themselves .	我們不需要一個大型的組織 , 讓它成為村民 。
and you probably hardly see a thai man there , it's always women , women , women , women .	你可能很難看到一個thai男人 , 女人、女人、女人、女人 。
and then we thought we'd help america , because america's been helping everyone , whether they want help or not .	接著 , 我們認為我們會幫助美國人 , 因為美國人都幫忙 , 不論他們想要幫助 。
and this is on the fourth of july .	這是在第四次 。
we decided to provide vasectomy to all men , but in particular , american men to the front of the queue , right up to the ambassador's residence during his [unclear] .	我們決定要提供給所有男性 , 但特別是美國人 , 到達亞巴斯大屠殺 。
and the hotel gave us the ballroom for it very appropriate room .	荷爾給了我們一個非常適合的房間 。
and since it was near lunch time , they said , " all right , we'll give you some lunch .	從那時起午餐時間 , 他們說: 「 好吧 , 我們會給你吃午餐 。
of course , it must be american cola .	當然 , 這一定是美國的煤炭 。
you get two brands , coke and pepsi .	你有兩種品牌、牛奶和棕色 。
and then the food is either hamburger or hotdog . "	食物是漢堡或熱門 。 」
and i thought a hotdog will be more symbolic .	我以為一個熱門會更具象徵性 。
and here is this , then , young man called willy bohm who worked for the usaid .	在這裡 , 這是這個 , 接著 , 年輕的年輕男士 , 叫做ybohm , 為美國援助組織 。
obviously , he's had his vasectomy because his hotdog is half eaten , and he was very happy .	很明顯地 , 他有他的陰莖 , 他很高興 。
it made a lot of news in america , and it angered some people also .	它在美國有許多新聞 , 有些人也很憤怒 。
i said , " don't worry . come over and i'll do the whole lot of you . "	我說: 「 別擔心 , 拜託 , 拜託 , 我來了 。 」
in all this thing , from seven children to 1 . 5 children , population growth rate of 3 . 3 to 0 . 5 .	從7個孩子到1.5個孩子 , 成長率是3.5個孩子 。
you could call it the cocacola approach if you like it was exactly the same thing .	你可以稱它為 「 卡柯拉方法 」 , 如果你喜歡它是一樣的東西 。
i'm not sure whether cocacola followed us , or we followed cocacola , but we're good friends .	我不確定卡卡卡卡哥拉 , 但我們是好朋友 。
and so that's the case of everyone joining in .	這就是每個人的喜悅 。
we didn't have a strong government . we didn't have lots of doctors .	我們沒有很強的政府 , 我們沒有很多的醫生 。
but it's everybody's job who can change attitude and behavior .	但 , 每個人都可以改變態度和行為 。
then aids came along and hit thailand , and we had to stop doing a lot of good things to fight aids .	接著 , 愛滋病出現了 , 我們必須停止做很多好事來對抗愛滋病 。
but unfortunately , the government was in denial , denial , denial .	但不幸的是 , 政府在密碼、密度、密度 。
so our work wasn't affected .	所以我們的工作並沒有影響 。
so i thought , " well , if you can't go to the government , go to the military . "	所以我想: 「 嗯 , 如果你不能去政府 , 去軍隊 。 」
so i went to the military and asked to borrow 300 radio stations .	於是我去了軍隊 , 請求借300台電台 。
