bad rules can prevent the kind of winwin solution that's available when people can bring new technologies in and make them available to someone like nelson .	糟糕的規則可以預防這種風力的解決方案 , 讓人們可以預防這種風力的解決方案 , 讓人們可以防止這種風力的解決方案 , 讓人們可以預防這種風力的解決方案 。
what kinds of rules ?	什麼規則呢 ?
the electric company in this nation operates under a rule , which says that it has to sell electricity at a very low , subsidized price in fact , a price that is so low it loses money on every unit that it sells .	在這個國家的電廠公司裡的電廠公司 , 會說 , 它需要賣出最低的價格 , 價格很低 , 價格很低 , 價格很低 , 價格相當低 。
so it has neither the resources , nor the incentives , to hook up many other users .	所以 , 不管有哪些資源 , 不管是資源 , 還沒用 , 還能用很多其他使用者 。
the president wanted to change this rule .	總統想要改變這個規則 。
he's seen that it's possible to have a different set of rules , rules where businesses earn a small profit , so they have an incentive to sign up more customers .	他看到了 , 這樣的規則是有可能有一種不同的規則 , 規則 , 商業賺錢 , 所以他們有很大的獎勵 , 讓更多客戶更客戶 。
that's the kind of rules that the cellphone company that nelson purchases his telephony from operates under .	這是一種規則 , 尼爾遜購買了他的手機公司 , 手機公司的執行長 ,
the president has seen how those rules worked well .	總統看過這些規則如何運作 。
so he tried to change the rules for pricing on electricity , but ran into a firestorm of protest from businesses and consumers who wanted to preserve the existing subsidized rates .	所以他試圖改變規則 , 以供應商業和消費者 , 希望保存這些規則 。
so he was stuck with rules that prevented him from letting the winwin solution help his country .	所以他被允許他用法律來幫助他的國家 。
and nelson is stuck studying under the streetlights .	nelson在街道上進行研究 。
the real challenge then , is to try to figure out how we can change rules .	真正的挑戰是 , 試圖找出我們如何改變規則 。
are there some rules we can develop for changing rules ?	有一些規則 , 我們能發展出改變規則嗎 ?
i want to argue that there is a general abstract insight that we can make practical , which is that , if we can give more choices to people , and more choices to leaders who , in many countries , are also people .	我想說的是 , 如果我們能給予更多的選擇 , 更多的選擇 , 去領導人 , 更多的選擇 , 也是人 。
but , it's useful to present the opposition between these two .	但 , 這兩者之間的反對是很有效的 。
because the kind of choice you might want to give to a leader , a choice like giving the president the choice to raise prices on electricity , takes away a choice that people in the economy want .	因為你可能想要給領袖的選擇 , 選擇要給一個領導者 , 選擇要給一個領導者 , 選擇要給領袖的選擇 , 例如 , 選擇要給領袖 , 選擇要給領袖的選擇 , 選擇要給領袖的選擇 。
they want the choice to be able to continue consuming subsidized electric power .	他們想要選擇能夠持續消費電力 。
so if you give just to one side or the other , you'll have tension or friction .	所以 , 如果你只給另一方 , 你就會有緊張或摩擦 。
but if we can find ways to give more choices to both , that will give us a set of rules for changing rules that get us out of traps .	但如果我們能找到方法 , 讓我們能找到方法 , 來改變規則 , 來改變規則 , 來改變規則 。
now , nelson also has access to the internet .	現在 , nelson也能取得網路 。

what haiti warns us is that rules can be bad because governments are weak .	海地的威脅是 , 我們的規則會很糟 , 因為政府很弱 。

now , china dramatically demonstrates both the potential and the challenges of working with rules .	現在 , 中國戲劇地展示了兩種潛力與規則的挑戰 。
back in the beginning of the data presented in this chart , china was the world's hightechnology leader .	在這個圖片中 , 中國是世界上最高科技的領導者 。
chinese had pioneered technologies like steel , printing , gunpowder .	中國有像鋼鐵、印刷、印刷、印刷的技術 。
but the chinese never adopted , at least in that period , effective rules for encouraging the spread of those ideas a profit motive that could have encouraged the spread .	但中國人從來沒有採用 , 至少在那段期間 , 有效的規則 , 可以鼓勵廣告傳播 。
and they soon adopted rules which slowed down innovation and cut china off from the rest of the world .	他們很快的規則慢慢下來 , 把中國從世界各地 。
so as other countries in the world innovated , in the sense both of developing newer technologies , but also developing newer rules , the chinese were cut off from those advances .	所以 , 其他國家在創新的國家 , 中國人也在發展新興的國家 , 但也開發新的規則 , 中國人會從這些進步開始 。
income there stayed stagnant , as it zoomed ahead in the rest of the world .	收入的保持穩定 , 世界各地的收入還不穩定 。

the brightest spot in china , which you can see on the edge of the outline here , is hong kong .	中國最亮的點子 , 你可以看到在線上 , 這裡是香港 。
hong kong was a small bit of china that , for most of the 20th century , operated under a very different set of rules than the rest of mainland china rules that were copied from working market economies of the time , and administered by the british .	首先 , 來自英國的中國規則 , 大約二十世紀中 , 中國的規則很少 , 由英國的規則所控制 。
in the 1950s , hong kong was a place where millions of people could go , from the mainland , to start in jobs like sewing shirts , making toys .	在1950年代 , 香港是個地方 , 有數百萬人可以從馬地開始工作 , 像是賣衣、玩具 。

hong kong was also the model which leaders like deng xiaoping could copy , when they decided to move all of the mainland towards the market model .	香港也是這樣的模式 , 當他們決定要搬到市場模式時 , 他們決定要搬到市場模式 。
but deng xiaoping instinctively understood the importance of offering choices to his people .	但 , 針對他人的重要性 , 來決定對他人的重要性 。
so instead of forcing everyone in china to shift immediately to the market model , they proceeded by creating some special zones that could do , in a sense , what britain did: make the opportunity to go work with the market rules available to the people who wanted to opt in there .	所以 , 不論是誰想要投入這個市場規則 , 讓大家能夠去工作 , 和市場規則 , 可以做到 , 來到市場規則 , 來到市場規則 , 讓大家能夠去工作 , 來到市場規則 , 來到市場規則 。
so they created four special economic zones around hong kong: zones where chinese could come and work , and cities grew up very rapidly there ; also zones where foreign firms could come in and make things .	所以他們創造了四個特別的經濟區塊 , 城市長大 , 城市長大 , 在那裡 , 城市長大 , 在那裡 , 城市長大 , 很快地 , 在那裡 , 城市長大 。
one of the zones next to hong kong has a city called shenzhen .	其中一個城市叫做nzhen 。
in that city there is a taiwanese firm that made the iphone that many of you have , and they made it with labor from chinese who moved there to shenzhen .	在這個城市裡 , 有一座城市有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 , 裡面有一座城市 ,
so after the four special zones , there were 14 coastal cites that were open in the same sense , and eventually demonstrated successes in these places that people could opt in to , that they flocked to because of the advantages they offered .	所以 , 在4個特區區 , 最後有14個災難 , 最終會讓人們可以選擇 , 讓人們可以選擇 , 因為他們所擁有的優勢 。
demonstrated successes there led to a consensus for a move toward the market model for the entire economy .	展示了成功 , 讓整個經濟體制變得更廣泛 。
now the chinese example shows us several points .	現在中國的例子顯示了我們幾個點 。
one is: preserve choices for people .	第一:保存選擇 。
two: operate on the right scale .	二:在正確的尺度上 。
if you try to change the rules in a village , you could do that , but a village would be too small to get the kinds of benefits you can get if you have millions of people all working under good rules .	如果你試著改變規則的規則 , 你就可以做到 , 但村子裡有數百萬人在一個村莊中做得很好 。
on the other hand , the nation is too big .	另一方面 , 國家太大了 。
if you try to change the rules in the nation , you can't give some people a chance to hold back , see how things turn out , and let others zoom ahead and try the new rules .	如果你試著改變規則 , 你不能給一些人一個機會 , 來看看如何轉變 , 讓其他人有機會 , 看看如何轉變 , 讓一些人有機會 , 看看如何轉變 , 讓其他人有機會 , 看看如何轉變 , 讓其他人有機會 , 看看如何轉變 , 讓一些人有機會 ,
but cities give you this opportunity to create new places , with new rules that people can opt in to .	但城市給你一個機會 , 創造新的地方 , 讓大家可以選擇 。
and they're large enough to get all of the benefits that we can have when millions of us work together under good rules .	他們很大 , 能夠得到所有我們能得到的好處 , 只要數百萬人一起合作 , 才能得到所有利益 。
so the proposal is that we conceive of something called a charter city .	因此 , 我們所謂的 「 慈善城市 」 。
we start with a charter that specifies all the rules required to attract the people who we'll need to build the city .	我們從一系列的規則開始 , 所有規則需要吸引我們所需要的人 , 才能建立城市 。
we'll need to attract the investors who will build out the infrastructure the power system , the roads , the port , the airport , the buildings .	我們需要吸引投資者 , 創造出基礎設施系統、道路、運動、機場、運動、機場 。
you'll need to attract firms , who will come hire the people who move there first .	你需要吸引人工 , 誰會僱用那些搬到哪裡的人 。
and you'll need to attract families , the residents who will come and live there permanently , raise their children , get an education for their children , and get their first job .	你需要吸引家庭 , 養育孩子們 , 教育給他們的孩子 , 她們的第一份工作 。
with that charter , people will move there .	有了這些圖片 , 人們會搬到那裡 。
the city can be built .	城市可以建造 。
and we can scale this model .	我們可以擴展這個模型 。
we can go do it over and over again .	我們可以再一次地做它 。
to make it work , we need good rules . we've already discussed that .	為了讓它運作 , 我們需要好的規則 , 我們已經討論了 。
those are captured in the charter .	這些被捕捉到 。
we also need the choices for people .	我們也需要選擇 。
that's really built into the model if we allow for the possibility of building cities on uninhabited land .	這真的是建立城市的基礎建設城市
you start from uninhabited territory .	你從未習慣的國家開始 。
people can come live under the new charter , but no one is forced to live under it .	人們可以生活在新的圖片中 , 但沒有人能被迫活在下面 。
the final thing we need are choices for leaders .	最後我們需要的選擇是領導者 。
and , to achieve the kind of choices we want for leaders we need to allow for the potential for partnerships between nations: cases where nations work together , in effect , de facto , the way china and britain worked together to build , first a little enclave of the market model , and then scale it throughout china .	為了達成我們想要的領導者 , 我們需要讓大家能參與其中的共同點:國家之間的合作 , 來建立 , 首先的市場模型 , 在中國和英國一起建立 , 首先 , 到中國和英國合作 。
in a sense , britain , inadvertently , through its actions in hong kong , did more to reduce world poverty than all the aid programs that we've undertaken in the last century .	在某種程度上 , 英國 , 無庸置疑的是 , 英國 , 在過去世紀中 , 沒有任何援助計畫 , 才能減少世界貧窮 。
so if we allow for these kind of partnerships to replicate this again , we can get those kinds of benefits scaled throughout the world .	所以 , 若我們能把這些夥伴重新複製 , 我們就能得到這些類型的益處在世界各地 。
in some cases this will involve a delegation of responsibility , a delegation of control from one country to another to take over certain kinds of administrative responsibilities .	在某些案例中 , 一個國家的負責任由一個國家的責任 , 來控制一個國家 , 另一個國家的責任 , 可以控制來自一個國家的責任 。
now , when i say that , some of you are starting to think , " well , is this just bringing back colonialism ? "	現在 , 當我說 , 你們當中有些人開始想: 「 嗯 , 這只是帶回殖民主義嗎 ? 」
it's not . but it's important to recognize that the kind of emotions that come up when we start to think about these things , can get in the way , can make us pull back , can shut down our ability , and our interest in trying to explore new ideas .	這不是 , 但很重要的是 , 要了解到當我們開始思考這些東西時 , 可以把我們帶回去 , 可以把我們的能力帶回去 , 並且我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 , 可以讓我們開始思考這些東西 。
why is this not like colonialism ?	為什麼不喜歡殖民主義 ?
the thing that was bad about colonialism , and the thing which is residually bad in some of our aid programs , is that it involved elements of coercion and condescension .	關於殖民主義 , 很糟糕的是 , 那些在我們的援助計畫中所做的 , 就是它涉入了許多援助計畫 。
this model is all about choices , both for leaders and for the people who will live in these new places .	這個模式是所有選擇 , 為了領導者 , 和那些住在這些新地方的人 。
and , choice is the antidote to coercion and condescension .	選擇是 「 解答 」 和 「 選擇 」 。
so let's talk about how this could play out in practice .	咱們來談談如何在練習中練習 。

it must have occurred to castro that he has the chance to do for cuba what deng xiaoping did for china , but he doesn't have a hong kong there on the island in cuba .	他必須有機會去做對中國 , 但他沒有一個洞穴在土地上 。

let us have a hong kong nearby .	咱們來談一下 。
some of my citizens will move into that city as well .	一些我的公民會搬進城市裡 。
others will hold back . but this will be the gateway that will connect the modern economy and the modern world to my country . "	其他人會再回來 , 但這會讓現代經濟和現代經濟和現代經濟和現代經濟現代化經濟和現代經濟現代化 。 」
now , where else might this model be tried ?	現在 , 其他可能發生在哪裡 ?
well , africa . i've talked with leaders in africa .	非洲 , 我和領導者在非洲 。
many of them totally get the notion of a special zone that people can opt into as a rule .	其中許多人都可以選擇成為一個規則 。
it's a rule for changing rules .	它是一種規則的規則 。
it's a way to create new rules , and let people optin without coercion , and the opposition that coercion can force .	它是一種創造新規則的方式 , 讓人們選擇 , 沒有勇氣 , 並且讓人們選擇 , 不用煤炭來創造新規則 。
they also totally get the idea that in some instances they can make more credible promises to longterm investors the kind of investors who will come build the port , build the roads , in a new city they can make more credible promises if they do it along with a partner nation .	他們也很清楚的承諾 , 在一個新的城市中 , 他們可以更清楚的承諾 , 可以讓更清楚的承諾 , 可以讓更清楚的承諾 , 可以讓更清楚的承諾 , 在他們能更清楚的承諾 , 在他們能做得更清楚的承諾 。
perhaps even in some arrangement that's a little bit like an escrow account , where you put land in the escrow account and the partner nation takes responsibility for it .	或許甚至在某些地方 , 有點像是一個退休金帳戶 , 你把土地放在垃圾帳戶中 , 把土地放在垃圾帳戶中 , 和夥伴合作夥伴國會負責 。

well , throughout the world , if we look at the lights at night , the one thing that's misleading is that , visually , it looks like most of the world is already built out .	嗯 , 在世界各地 , 如果我們觀察燈光在夜晚 , 它看起來像大部分都已經建造出來的 。

if you move the dots down to the bottom of the rectangle you can see that the cities for the existing three billion urban residents take up only three percent of the arable land on earth .	如果你把海底下降到最底層的地位 , 你可以看到這個城市 , 地球上只有三分之三十億的城市 。
so if we wanted to build cities for another billion people , they would be dots like this .	所以如果我們想要建立城市 , 數十億人 , 他們就會像這樣 。

we'd dramatically reduce the human footprint on earth by building more cities that people can move to .	我們會大幅地減少人類足跡 , 讓大家可以移動到地球上 。
and if these are cities governed by good rules , they can be cities where people are safe from crime , safe from disease and bad sanitation , where people have a chance to get a job .	如果這些城市被好規則 , 他們可以成為城市 , 人們有機會去工作 , 才能得到工作 。

so what will it take to get started building the first charter cities , scaling this so we build many more ?	所以 , 要開始建造第一張圖片 , 我們建造了第一張圖片 , 我們建造了什麼 ?
it would help to have a manual .	它會幫助有人性 。

how would we finance this ?	我們要如何定義這個 ?
turns out singapore and hong kong are cities that made huge gains on the value of the land that they owned when they got started .	結果發現 , 土地和香港是城市的價值 , 讓大量的價值歸功於他們所擁有的價值 。
you could use the gains on the value of the land to pay for things like the police , the courts , but the school system and the health care system too , which make this a more attractive place to live , makes this a place where people have higher incomes which , incidentally , makes the land more valuable .	你可以用這塊土地的價值 , 讓土地變得更有吸引力 , 但學校系統和醫療保健系統 , 讓它變得更有吸引力 , 讓土地更有吸引力 , 讓土地更有價值 。
so the incentives for the people helping to construct this zone and build it , and set up the basic rules , go very much in the right direction .	所以 , 人們協助建構這個區塊 , 並建立基礎規則 , 以正確方向為基礎規則 。
so there are many other details like this .	還有許多其他細節 。
how could we have buildings that are low cost and affordable for people who work in a first job , assembling something like an iphone , but make those buildings energy efficient , and make sure that they are safe , so they don't fall down in an earthquake or a hurricane .	我們要如何建造能源效率 , 讓這些建築物能有效率地震 , 並且確保它們是安全的 , 但讓這些建築物能有效率地震 , 並且確保它們是安全的 , 所以它們不會落在地震或颶風 。

let me conclude with this picture .	讓我結論這張照片 。
the reason we can be so well off , even though there is so many people on earth , is because of the power of ideas .	我們很快就知道的原因是 , 儘管有許多人在地球上 , 是因為有權力的想法 。
we can share ideas with other people , and when they discover them , they share with us .	我們可以分享和其他人分享的想法 , 當他們發現他們 , 他們和我們分享 。
it's not like scarce objects , where sharing means we each get less .	它不像恐怖的物品 , 分享的意思是 , 我們每次都比較少 。
when we share ideas we all get more .	當我們分享想法時 , 我們都能得到更多 。
when we think about ideas in that way , we usually think about technologies .	當我們思考這些想法時 , 我們通常會想到科技 。
but there is another class of ideas: the rules that govern how we interact with each other ; rules like , let's have a tax system that supports a research university that gives away certain kinds of knowledge for free .	但還有另一個課題:規則:規則:規則:規則我們如何互相彼此交互作用 , 我們有另一項規則:規則 , 我們來提供一些關於免費的規則 。
let's have a system where we have ownership of land that is registered in a government office , that people can pledge as collateral .	讓我們有一個系統 , 在政府辦公室裡 , 人們可以帶領土地進入政府辦公室 。
if we can keep innovating on our space of rules , and particularly innovate in the sense of coming up with rules for changing rules , so we don't get stuck with bad rules , then we can keep moving progress forward and truly make the world a better place , so that people like nelson and his friends don't have to study any longer under the streetlights . thank you .	如果我們能持續創新 , 透過規則來改變規則 , 我們就可以繼續進步 , 讓世界變得更好 , 所以 , 像nelson和他的朋友 , 不需要研究任何在街道上的規則 。 謝謝 。
genomics pioneer craig venter takes a break from his epic roundtheworld expedition to talk about the millions of genes his team has discovered so far in its quest to map the ocean’s biodiversity .	基因組成員的基因組已經發現了 , 遠遠超過了數百萬個基因組成員 , 他的基因組發現了 , 遠離他的隊伍 , 發現了很遠的遠遠 , 去地地地地地地地地地地地地地圖海洋生物多樣性 。
dna , biosphere , biotech , entrepreneur , genetics , invention , oceans , science , technology	dna , 生物科技 , 生物科技 , 生物科技 , 生物科技 , 生物科技 , 生物科技 , 生物學家 , 生物科技 。
craig venter on dna and the sea	dna和海裡的dna和海洋 。
at the break , i was asked by several people about my comments about the aging debate .	突破時 , 我被問到我對辯論的評論 。
and this will be my only comment on it .	這是我唯一的評論 。
and that is , i understand that optimists greatly outlive pessimists .	那就是 , 我了解 , 樂觀主義者很樂觀 。
what i'm going to tell you about in my 18 minutes is how we're about to switch from reading the genetic code to the first stages of beginning to write the code ourselves .	我現在要告訴各位的是 , 18分鐘內 , 我們如何從閱讀基因編碼開始寫程式碼 。
it's only 10 years ago this month when we published the first sequence of a freeliving organism , that of haemophilus influenzae .	只有十年前 , 我們發表出版了第一個序列的免疫系統 , 叫做 「 愛滋病菌 」 。
that took a genome project from 13 years down to four months .	這個基因組計畫從13年到4個月 。
we can now do that same genome project in the order of two to eight hours .	我們現在可以做同樣的基因組計畫 , 兩到八個小時 。
so in the last decade , a large number of genomes have been added: most human pathogens , a couple of plants , several insects and several mammals , including the human genome .	在過去十年中 , 許多基因組成了最人類的基因組 , 包括人類基因組 。
genomics at this stage of the thinking from a little over 10 years ago was , by the end of this year , we might have between three and five genomes sequenced ; it's on the order of several hundred .	在這個十年前 , 我們可能有三到五個基因組序列的基因組序列 , 大概是幾百個基因組 。
we just got a grant from the gordon and betty moore foundation to sequence 130 genomes this year , as a side project from environmental organisms .	我們剛剛從gordon和betmoore基金會找到了130個基因組 , 其中一個來自環境生物的基因組 。
so the rate of reading the genetic code has changed .	閱讀基因編碼已經改變了 。
but as we look , what's out there , we've barely scratched the surface on what is available on this planet .	但當我們看 , 到底發生了什麼 , 我們就在這個星球上找到了這個星球的表面 。
most people don't realize it , because they're invisible , but microbes make up about a half of the earth's biomass , whereas all animals only make up about one onethousandth of all the biomass .	大部分的人都不了解它 , 因為它們是可見的 , 但微生物學家 , 所有動物都只佔了地球生物數量的三分之一 。
and maybe it's something that people in oxford don't do very often , but if you ever make it to the sea , and you swallow a mouthful of seawater , keep in mind that each milliliter has about a million bacteria and on the order of 10 million viruses .	可能是人們在牛津不做的事 , 但如果你把它們帶到海水中 , 每一千萬個細菌 , 都有一百萬個細菌 , 一百萬個細菌 。
less than 5 , 000 microbial species have been characterized as of two years ago , and so we decided to do something about it .	超過50000種微生物物種已經成為兩年前 , 所以我們決定要做點什麼 。
and we started the sorcerer ii expedition , where we were , as with great oceanographic expeditions , trying to sample the ocean every 200 miles .	然後我們開始了武器工程師 , 試圖採取海洋各樣的海洋 , 每200英哩 。
we started in bermuda for our test project , then moved up to halifax , working down the u . s . east coast , the caribbean sea , the panama canal , through to the galapagos , then across the pacific , and we're in the process now of working our way across the indian ocean .	我們開始在加勒比海岸 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 美國東岸 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 美國東岸 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 美國東岸 , 加勒比海 , 加勒比海 , 美國東岸 。
it's very tough duty ; we're doing this on a sailing vessel , in part to help excite young people about going into science .	這是非常艱難的 。 我們正在做這個 , 一趟旅行 , 讓年輕人去探索科學 。
the experiments are incredibly simple .	實驗非常簡單 。
we just take seawater and we filter it , and we collect different size organisms on different filters , and then take their dna back to our lab in rockville , where we can sequence a hundred million letters of the genetic code every 24 hours .	我們把dna送到我們的實驗室裡 , 我們收集不同的濾水器 , 然後把dna送到我們的實驗室 , 我們收集不同的濾水器 , 然後把它們dna送到我們的實驗室 , 我們收集了不同的濾水 , 然後把它們dna回到我們的實驗室 , 我們收集了不同的濾水器 , 然後把它們dna送到我們的實驗室 , 我們收集了不同的濾水器 , 然後把它們dna回到我們的實驗室 , 我們收集了不同的濾水
and with doing this , we've made some amazing discoveries .	這樣做 , 我們做了一些驚人的發現 。
for example , it was thought that the visual pigments that are in our eyes there was only one or two organisms in the environment that had these same pigments .	舉例來說 , 我們眼睛中只有一個或兩個有機體的視覺色素 。
it turns out , almost every species in the upper parts of the ocean in warm parts of the world have these same photoreceptors , and use sunlight as the source of their energy and communication .	結果發現 , 幾乎每種物種都在海洋中 , 有著相同的光源 , 利用陽光來源於能量和溝通之中 。
from one site , from one barrel of seawater , we discovered 1 . 3 million new genes and as many as 50 , 000 new species .	從一個地方 , 我們發現了1.3百萬個新基因 , 其中有150 , 000種新的基因 。
we've extended this to the air now with a grant from the sloan foundation .	我們已經擴展到這個空氣 , 來自土地基金會 。
we're measuring how many viruses and bacteria all of us are breathing in and out every day , particularly on airplanes or closed auditoriums .	我們測量了多少病毒和細菌 , 每天都有呼吸 , 特別是在飛機或閉上 。
we filter through some simple apparatuses ; we collect on the order of a billion microbes from just a day filtering on top of a building in new york city .	我們收集了一些簡單的應用程式 , 我們收集了幾十億個微生物 , 僅僅是紐約市的頂端 。
and we're in the process of sequencing all that at the present time .	我們現在正在處理這些過程 。
just on the data collection side , just where we are through the galapagos , we're finding that almost every 200 miles , we see tremendous diversity in the samples in the ocean .	僅僅在資料集中 , 我們發現幾乎每200英哩 , 我們發現幾乎每百英哩 , 我們發現幾乎每百英哩 , 我們發現幾乎每百英哩 , 我們發現幾乎每百公里 , 我們發現幾乎每百公里的多樣性 。
some of these make logical sense , in terms of different temperature gradients .	有些會產生邏輯 , 不同溫度升級 。
so this is a satellite photograph based on temperatures red being warm , blue being cold and we found there's a tremendous difference between the warm water samples and the cold water samples , in terms of abundant species .	這是一張衛星照片 , 由溫暖的溫暖藍色 , 我們發現那裡有很大的差異 , 包括溫暖和寒冷的水樣 , 和寒冷的水樣 , 我們發現有很大的差異 。
the other thing that surprised us quite a bit is these photoreceptors detect different wavelengths of light , and we can predict that based on their amino acid sequence .	另外一件令人驚訝的是 , 我們可以預測它們的微小組合 , 可以預測它們的原始序列 。
and these vary tremendously from region to region .	這些從區域到區域的區域 。
maybe not surprisingly , in the deep ocean , where it's mostly blue , the photoreceptors tend to see blue light .	或許不令人驚訝的是 , 在深海中 , 在深海中 , 最藍光的部分是藍光 。
when there's a lot of chlorophyll around , they see a lot of green light .	那裡有許多綠光 , 它們會看到很多綠光 。
but they vary even more , possibly moving towards infrared and ultraviolet in the extremes .	但他們甚至更加入侵 , 甚至更有可能在極端中扮演的角色 。
just to try and get an assessment of what our gene repertoire was , we assembled all the data including all of ours thus far from the expedition , which represents more than half of all the gene data on the planet and it totaled around 29 million genes .	為了嘗試 , 我們把所有的資料包含所有資料 , 包括我們所有的基因資料 , 我們組成了所有的資料 , 包含了我們所有的資料 , 包括我們所有的資料 , 包括我們所有的基因資料 , 大約29萬個基因資料 。
and we tried to put these into gene families to see what these discoveries are: are we just discovering new members of known families , or are we discovering new families ?	我們試圖把這些發現新成的家庭 , 或我們發現新的家庭 , 或我們發現了新的家庭 ?
and it turns out we have about 50 , 000 major gene families , but every new sample we take in the environment adds in a linear fashion to these new families .	結果發現 , 我們有大約五萬個主要的基因家庭 , 但每種新的家庭 , 我們都有大約有五萬個主要基因家庭 。
so we're at the earliest stages of discovery about basic genes , components and life on this planet .	所以 , 我們在這個星球上發現最早的階段 , 是關於基本基因、元素和生命 。
when we look at the socalled evolutionary tree , we're up on the upper righthand corner with the animals .	當我們觀察到 「 人類 」 的 「 人類 」 時 , 我們就在 「 人類 」 的角度上 。
of those roughly 29 million genes , we only have around 24 , 000 in our genome .	大約29萬個基因組中 , 我們只有29萬個基因組 。
and if you take all animals together , we probably share less than 30 , 000 and probably maybe a dozen or more thousand different gene families .	如果你把所有的動物聚在一起 , 我們可能有超過三萬個不同的基因家庭 。
i view that these genes are now not only the design components of evolution .	我看到這些基因現在不是唯一的設計元素 。
and we think in a genecentric view maybe going back to richard dawkins' ideas than in a genomecentric view , which are different constructs of these gene components .	我們認為 , 在基因組合中有不同的建構 , 這些基因組成的基因組合 。
synthetic dna , the ability to synthesize dna , has changed at sort of the same pace that dna sequencing has over the last decade or two , and is getting very rapid and very cheap .	合成dna的基因組成dna序列 , 在過去十年或兩年之間 , 基因組成dna序列非常便宜 。
our first thought about synthetic genomics came when we sequenced the second genome back in 1995 , and that from mycoplasma genitalium .	我們第一次想到合成基因組學會發生在1995年 , 我們第一次想到合成基因組 , 我們第一次想到合成基因組 。
and we have really nice tshirts that say , you know , " i heart my genitalium . "	我們有很棒的t恤 , 說: 「 我心臟 。 」
this is actually just a microorganism .	這只是一個微生物 。
but it has roughly 500 genes .	但它大約有500個基因 。
haemophilus had 1 , 800 genes .	漢菲爾斯有1、800個基因 。
and we simply asked the question , if one species needs 800 , another 500 , is there a smaller set of genes that might comprise a minimal operating system ?	我們只問這個問題 , 如果一個物種需要800 , 500 , 另一個500 , 另一個500 , 另一個500 , 另一個500 , 另一個500 , 另一個500個物種需要800 , 另一個500 , 另一個500個物種需要800 , 另一個500 , 另一個500個 ,
so we started doing transposon mutagenesis .	所以 , 我們開始做轉變的突變 。
transposons are just small pieces of dna that randomly insert in the genetic code .	翻譯只是小小的dna , 在基因編碼中被遺傳編碼 。
and if they insert in the middle of the gene , they disrupt its function .	如果他們在基因中中間 , 它們會破壞它的功能 。
so we made a map of all the genes that could take transposon insertions and we called those " nonessential genes . "	所以我們做了一張地圖 , 把所有基因的基因組成 , 叫做 「 基因 」 。
but it turns out the environment is very critical for this , and you can only define an essential or nonessential gene based on exactly what's in the environment .	但結果發現 , 環境非常關鍵 , 你只能定義一個特質或基因基礎在環境中 。
we also tried to take a more directly intellectual approach with the genomes of 13 related organisms , and we tried to compare all of those , to see what they had in common .	我們也試著用更直接的智慧方法 , 和基因組合約13個聯合體的基因組 , 我們試著用更直接的智慧方法 , 和基因組結合在一起 , 我們試著用更直接的智慧方法來處理這些基因組 。
and we got these overlapping circles . and we found only 173 genes common to all 13 organisms .	然後我們發現只有173個基因共通 , 只有173個基因共通 。
the pool expanded a little bit if we ignored one intracellular parasite ; it expanded even more when we looked at core sets of genes of around 310 or so .	若我們忽略了一組基因 , 就會擴大 , 只要我們分析到大約310個元素 , 就會擴大 。
so we think that we can expand or contract genomes , depending on your point of view here , to maybe 300 to 400 genes from the minimal of 500 .	所以我們認為我們可以擴大或複製基因組 , 或收縮基因組 , 大約300個基因組 , 大約是500個基因組 。
the only way to prove these ideas was to construct an artificial chromosome with those genes in them , and we had to do this in a cassettebased fashion .	唯一能證明這些想法是要建立一個人工染色體 , 我們必須做這個點子 , 來建立一個人工染色體 。
we found that synthesizing accurate dna in large pieces was extremely difficult .	我們發現合成精確的dna是非常困難的 。
ham smith and clyde hutchison , my colleagues on this , developed an exciting new method that allowed us to synthesize a 5 , 000base pair virus in only a twoweek period that was 100 percent accurate , in terms of its sequence and its biology .	哈姆•史密斯 , 和我的同事 , 研發出一種令人興奮的新方法 , 讓我們能夠合成5 , 000個鹼基酸鹼基對它的序列和生物學 。
it was a quite exciting experiment when we just took the synthetic piece of dna , injected it in the bacteria and all of a sudden , that dna started driving the production of the virus particles that turned around and then killed the bacteria .	這是一項令人興奮的實驗 , 當我們把病毒粒子聚在一起時 , dna會開始驅使病毒粒子進入細菌 , 然後殺害細菌 。
this was not the first synthetic virus a polio virus had been made a year before but it was only one tenthousandth as active and it took three years to do .	這不是第一個合成病毒的病毒 , 它花了三年的時間才完成 。
this is a cartoon of the structure of phi x 174 .	這是194年的卡通圖 。
this is a case where the software now builds its own hardware , and that's the notions that we have with biology .	這是軟體製造出自己的硬體 , 那就是我們有生物學的概念 。
people immediately jump to concerns about biological warfare , and i had recent testimony before a senate committee , and a special committee the u . s . government has set up to review this area .	人們馬上就開始重新審查這個區域 , 我最近在參議院委員會議委員會議員 , 特別委員會在委員會議中 , 去審查這個區域 。
and i think it's important to keep reality in mind , versus what happens with people's imaginations .	我認為 , 要保持現實 , 和人們想像力的想像力很重要 。
basically , any virus that's been sequenced today that genome can be made .	基本上 , 任何病毒都被編碼成的病毒 。
and people immediately freak out about things about ebola or smallpox , but the dna from this organism is not infective .	人們馬上對伊波拉或小小的基因組合 , 但dna從這個機體中沒有感染 。
so even if somebody made the smallpox genome , that dna itself would not cause infections .	所以即使某人製造了微小的基因組 , dna本身不會造成感染 。
the real concern that security departments have is designer viruses .	真正的安全部門是設計病毒 。
and there's only two countries , the u . s . and the former soviet union , that had major efforts on trying to create biological warfare agents .	只有兩個國家 , 美國和前蘇聯盟 , 和前蘇聯盟合作 , 創造生物戰法 。
if that research is truly discontinued , there should be very little activity on the knowhow to make designer viruses in the future .	如果研究是真正的突破 , 應該要讓設計師病毒在未來中更有趣 。
i think singlecell organisms are possible within two years .	我認為單細胞機體已經有可能兩年了 。
and possibly eukaryotic cells , those that we have , are possible within a decade .	可能性細胞 , 在十年內 , 我們已經有的可能性 。
so we're now making several dozen different constructs , because we can vary the cassettes and the genes that go into this artificial chromosome .	所以我們現在已經做了幾十個不同的建構 , 因為我們可以把這些特質和基因放進這個人工染色體中 。
the key is , how do you put all of the others ?	關鍵是 , 你如何把所有其他東西帶給其他人 ?
we start with these fragments , and then we have a homologous recombination system that reassembles those into a chromosome .	我們從這些碎片開始 , 然後我們有了一個巨大的組合系統 , 將這些碎片重新組合起來 。
this is derived from an organism , deinococcus radiodurans , that can take three million rads of radiation and not be killed .	這是從機體中有機體的durans , 可以拿三百萬隻蚊子 , 沒有殺害 。
it reassembles its genome after this radiation burst in about 12 to 24 hours , after its chromosomes are literally blown apart .	它的基因組成立了24小時 , 在這個輻射後的基因組排序之後 , 染色體的基因組會被分裂 。
this organism is ubiquitous on the planet , and exists perhaps now in outer space due to all our travel there .	這個機體在地球上有機體 , 存在可能在外太空中 , 存在於我們行星上 。
this is a glass beaker after about half a million rads of radiation .	這是一張玻璃底下 , 大約有5000萬個雷射輻射 。
the glass started to burn and crack , while the microbes sitting in the bottom just got happier and happier .	玻璃開始燃燒和破裂 , 而微生物在底部的微生物會變得更快樂、更快樂 。
here's an actual picture of what happens: the top of this shows the genome after 1 . 7 million rads of radiation .	這是一張圖片 , 結果顯示出了基因組 , 在1.7百萬次輻射 。
the chromosome is literally blown apart .	染色體其實是很明顯的 。
and here's that same dna automatically reassembled 24 hours later .	同樣的dna自動化合成24小時後 。
it's truly stunning that these organisms can do that , and we probably have thousands , if not tens of thousands , of different species on this planet that are capable of doing that .	真正的發現這些生物可以做到 , 我們可能有數千個物種 , 可能有數以千計的物種 , 可能有數以千計的物種 。
after these genomes are synthesized , the first step is just transplanting them into a cell without a genome .	在這些基因組合成之後 , 第一步只是把它們變成細胞沒有基因組 。
so we think synthetic cells are going to have tremendous potential , not only for understanding the basis of biology but for hopefully environmental and society issues .	所以我們認為合成細胞將會有巨大的潛力 , 不僅能理解生物學的基礎 , 還能帶來巨大的潛力 , 也不只能了解生物學的基礎 , 以及社會議題 。
for example , from the third organism we sequenced , methanococcus jannaschii it lives in boiling water temperatures ; its energy source is hydrogen and all its carbon comes from co2 it captures back from the environment .	舉例來說 , 二氧化碳來自二氧化碳 , 碳來自於環境的二氧化碳 。
so we know lots of different pathways , thousands of different organisms now that live off of co2 , and can capture that back .	所以我們知道許多不同路徑 , 數以千計的生物 , 可以捕捉到它 。
so instead of using carbon from oil for synthetic processes , we have the chance of using carbon and capturing it back from the atmosphere , converting that into biopolymers or other products .	所以 , 利用碳從大氣層開始吸收 , 將它從大氣層吸收到生物聚合物 , 或其他產品 。
we have one organism that lives off of carbon monoxide , and we use as a reducing power to split water to produce hydrogen and oxygen .	我們有一種有機體 , 生活在碳化氫和氧氣中 , 我們使用的能量來製造氫和氧氣 。
also , there's numerous pathways that can be engineered metabolizing methane .	還有許多路徑 , 可以用來製造出甲烷 。
and dupont has a major program with statoil in norway to capture and convert the methane from the gas fields there into useful products .	由石油來捕捉 , 將甲烷從氣體中轉換成有用的材料 。
within a short while , i think there's going to be a new field called " combinatorial genomics , " because with these new synthesis capabilities , these vast gene array repertoires and the homologous recombination , we think we can design a robot to make maybe a million different chromosomes a day .	在短期內 , 我認為 , 我們認為我們可以設計一個機器人 , 來創造一種新領域 , 叫做 「 基因組合體 」 , 因為這些新領域叫做 「 基因組合體 」 , 因為這些新領域叫做 「 基因組合體 」 , 因為這些新領域 , 我們認為我們可以設計一個機器人 , 來製造出一百萬種不同的染色體 。
and therefore , as with all biology , you get selection through screening , whether you're screening for hydrogen production , or chemical production , or just viability .	因此 , 所有生物學 , 都可以通過螢幕 , 不論你是如何製造或化學產品 , 或化學產品 , 或化學產品 。
to understand the role of these genes is going to be well within reach .	為了了解這些基因的重要性 , 一定會很有趣 。
we're trying to modify photosynthesis to produce hydrogen directly from sunlight .	我們正在嘗試改造從太陽光合作來產生氫氣的作用 。
photosynthesis is modulated by oxygen , and we have an oxygeninsensitive hydrogenase that we think will totally change this process .	光合作是氧氣 , 我們有氧氣濃度的氫氣 , 我們認為會完全改變這個過程 。
we're also combining cellulases , the enzymes that break down complex sugars into simple sugars and fermentation in the same cell for producing ethanol .	我們也結合了細胞的酵素 , 酵素分裂成簡單的糖和酵素 , 酵素分裂成簡單的糖和酵素 , 酵素分裂成簡單的糖和酵素 。
pharmaceutical production is already under way in major laboratories using microbes .	藥物生產已經在主要實驗室使用微生物 。
the chemistry from compounds in the environment is orders of magnitude more complex than our best chemists can produce .	在環境裡的化學 , 比我們最佳化學家所能製造出的化學還要複雜 。
i think future engineered species could be the source of food , hopefully a source of energy , environmental remediation and perhaps replacing the petrochemical industry .	我認為未來的工程是食物的源源 , 可能是食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 , 希望能成為食物的源源 。
let me just close with ethical and policy studies .	讓我和政策研究有關 。
we delayed the start of our experiments in 1999 until we completed a yearandahalf bioethical review as to whether we should try and make an artificial species .	我們在1999年開始進行實驗 , 直到我們完成了一整年的實驗 , 直到我們完成了一個人工物種 。
every major religion participated in this .	每個主要宗教都參與這個 。

psychologist philip zimbardo says happiness and success are rooted in a trait most of us disregard: the way we orient toward the past , present and future . he suggests we calibrate our outlook on time as a first step to improving our lives .	心理學家philipzimbardo會說幸福和成功是我們第一次步步改善我們的生活方式 。

life is temptation . it's all about yielding , resisting , yes , no , now , later , impulsive , reflective , present focus and future focus .	生命是無所不在的 , 反思、反思、反思、反思、反思、反思、反思 , 及未來的焦點 。

now lets tempt fouryearolds , giving them a treat .	現在讓我們嘗試四歲的孩子 , 給他們一個治療 。
they can have one marshmallow now . but if they wait until the experimenter comes back , they can have two .	牠們可以有一隻馬鈴薯 , 但如果他們等直到實驗人員回來 , 他們就會有兩隻 。

walter mischel , my colleague at stanford , went back 14 years later , to try to discover what was different about those kids .	史丹佛大學的同事 , 我在史丹佛大學的同事 , 試圖發現對這些孩子有什麼不同 。
there were enormous differences between kids who resisted and kids who yielded , in many ways .	孩子們有很大的差異 , 在許多方面都有很大的差異 。
the kids who resisted scored 250 points higher on the sat .	拯救了250位更高的孩子 。
that's enormous . that's like a whole set of different iq points .	這很龐大 , 有點像是一整套不同的智商 。
they didn't get in as much trouble . they were better students .	他們沒有被困惑 , 他們是比較好的學生 。
they were selfconfident and determined . and the key for me today , the key for you , is , they were futurefocused rather than presentfocused .	他們有自信和決心 , 今天的關鍵是 , 我今天的鑰匙是 , 你的關鍵是 , 他們是自信和決心 , 而今天的關鍵是 , 他們是自信和決定 , 而現在是我的關鍵 。
so what is time perspective ? that's what i'm going to talk about today .	所以 , 我今天要談的是什麼 ? 這是我今天要談的 。
time perspective is the study of how individuals , all of us , divide the flow of your human experience into time zones or time categories .	觀點是 , 人類體驗的研究 , 或時間分裂 , 或時間分裂 。
and you do it automatically and nonconsciously .	然後你會自動地和非意識的 。
they vary between cultures , between nations , between individuals , between social classes , between education levels .	在社會階級之間 , 社會階級之間 , 社會階級之間之間的差異 。
and the problem is that they can become biased , because you learn to overuse some of them and underuse the others .	問題是 , 他們會變得偏見 , 因為你學會把它們分裂成偏見 , 因為你學會把它們分裂成偏見 。
what determines any decision you make ?	決定你做了什麼決定 ?
you make a decision on which you're going to base an action .	你做出決定 , 你要做一個決定 。
for some people it's only about what is in the immediate situation , what other people are doing and what you're feeling .	有些人在做的事 , 其他人正在做的事 , 以及你所感受的 。
and those people , when they make their decisions in that format we're going to call them " presentoriented , " because their focus is what is now .	那些人 , 當他們做出決策時 , 我們會稱他們為 「 現代 」 , 因為他們的焦點是現在 。
for others , the present is irrelevant .	對於其他人來說 , 情況是不相關的 。
it's always about " what is this situation like that i've experienced in the past ? "	它總是會說: 「 我在過去的情況是什麼樣子 ? 」
so that their decisions are based on past memories .	他們的決策是基於過去記憶 。
and we're going to call those people " pastoriented , " because they focus on what was .	我們會稱這些人為 「 過去 」 因為他們焦點放在哪裡
for others it's not the past , it's not the present , it's only about the future .	對其他人來說 , 它不是過去 , 而是未來 。
their focus is always about anticipated consequences .	他們的焦點是關於預期的後果 。
we're going to call them " futureoriented . " their focus is on what will be .	我們會稱他們為 「 未來 」 , 他們的焦點是未來 。
so , time paradox , i want to argue , the paradox of time perspective , is something that influences every decision you make , you're totally unaware of .	所以 , 時間矛盾 , 我想要說 , 矛盾是 , 所有決定你所做的事 , 你完全不了解 。
namely , the extent to which you have one of these biased time perspectives .	意思是 , 你有這種偏見的觀點 。
well there is actually six of them . there are two ways to be presentoriented .	其中有兩種方式 , 可以有兩種方式 。
there is two ways to be pastoriented , two ways to be future .	有兩種方式可以成為未來 。
you can focus on pastpositive , or pastnegative .	你可以專注在正面上 , 或負面 。
you can be presenthedonistic , namely you focus on the joys of life , or presentfatalist it doesn't matter , your life is controlled .	你可以說是 「 生命 」 的喜悅 , 意思是 , 你的生活被控制 。
you can be futureoriented , setting goals .	你可以成為未來 , 創造目標 。
or you can be transcendental future: namely , life begins after death .	或者 , 生命是從死亡後開始的 。
developing the mental flexibility to shift time perspectives fluidly depending on the demands of the situation , that's what you've got to learn to do .	發展出心理的責任 , 要學習要做的事 , 那就是你必須學習的事 。
so , very quickly , what is the optimal time profile ?	所以 , 很快的 , 什麼是最樂觀的呢 ?
high on pastpositive . moderately high on future .	高於未來的高度 。
and moderate on presenthedonism .	而在現代主義中 , 現代主義 。
and always low on pastnegative and presentfatalism .	總是低於負面和真實主義 。
so the optimal temporal mix is what you get from the past pastpositive gives you roots . you connect your family , identity and your self .	所以最基本的混合是你從過去的直覺到你的家人、身分和你的自身 。
what you get from the future is wings to soar to new destinations , new challenges .	你從未來所得到的 , 新的挑戰 , 新的挑戰 。
what you get from the present hedonism is the energy , the energy to explore yourself , places , people , sensuality .	你所得到的能量是能量 , 能探索自己、人、人、感覺 。
any time perspective in excess has more negatives than positives .	任何時間都比正面更負面 。
what do futures sacrifice for success ?	未來犧牲了成功 ?
they sacrifice family time . they sacrifice friend time .	他們犧牲了家庭的時間 , 犧牲了家人 。
they sacrifice fun time . they sacrifice personal indulgence .	他們犧牲了個人的成年 。
they sacrifice hobbies . and they sacrifice sleep . so it affects their health .	他們犧牲睡眠 , 所以它會影響健康 。
and they live for work , achievement and control .	他們活著工作、成就和控制 。
i'm sure that resonates with some of the tedsters .	我肯定會和一些tedstersterstersterster 。
and it resonated for me . i grew up as a poor kid in the south bronx ghetto , a sicilian family everyone lived in the past and present .	對我來說 , 我生長在南布朗克斯加坡 , 一個貧困的孩子 , 在南布朗克斯加坡 , 一個貧困的孩子 , 當時在南布朗克斯 , 一個貧困的孩子 。
i'm here as a futureoriented person who went over the top , who did all these sacrifices because teachers intervened , and made me future oriented .	我是一位在前面的人 , 他們做了所有這些犧牲 , 因為老師們介入 , 並且讓我更為未來 。
told me don't eat that marshmallow , because if you wait you're going to get two of them , until i learned to balance out .	告訴我不要吃香菸 , 因為如果你等待你等待你等待你會得到兩位 , 直到我學到平衡 。
i've added presenthedonism , i've added a focus on the pastpositive , so , at 76 years old , i am more energetic than ever , more productive , and i'm happier than i have ever been .	我已經加入了專注 , 在76年之前 , 我比起更有生產力的 , 我更有生產力 , 我比以前更有更精彩 , 更有生產力 。
i just want to say that we are applying this to many world problems: changing the dropout rates of school kids , combating addictions , enhancing teen health , curing vets' ptsd with time metaphors getting miracle cures promoting sustainability and conservation , reducing physical rehabilitation where there is a 50percent drop out rate , altering appeals to suicidal terrorists , and modifying family conflicts as timezone clashes .	我只想說 , 我們正在應用在許多世界問題上:改變了學校的孩子、結婚 , 及保育 , 和保育 , 和保育 , 改善了永續發展 , 及保育 , 增加了數量 , 改善各式各樣的家庭衝突 , 及保育 , 增加了五分之一 , 增加了數量 , 改善了永續發展 , 及保育 , 讓許多世界問題改變 。

now , the saturn system is a rich planetary system .	現在 , 土星系統是一個豐富的星體系統 。
it offers mystery , scientific insight and obviously splendor beyond compare , and the investigation of this system has enormous cosmic reach .	它提供了神秘、科學洞見 , 和明顯的調查 , 由於這個系統有巨大的宇宙 。
in fact , just studying the rings alone , we stand to learn a lot about the discs of stars and gas that we call the spiral galaxies .	事實上 , 只是研究我們所謂的恆星和氣體我們稱之為 「 太空星系 」
and here's a beautiful picture of the andromeda nebula , which is our closest , largest spiral galaxy to the milky way .	這裡有個美麗的圖片 , 這是我們最接近的 , 最大的星系 , 與銀河系 。
and then , here's a beautiful composite of the whirlpool galaxy , taken by the hubble space telescope .	然後 , 這裡有個美麗的成果 , 由哈伯太空望遠鏡所拍攝的 。
so the journey back to saturn is really part of and is also a metaphor for a much larger human voyage to understand the interconnectedness of everything around us , and also how humans fit into that picture .	所以 , 回到土星的旅程 , 也是一個更大的人類 , 來了解我們周圍的周圍 , 以及人類如何形成這個圖片 。
and it pains me that i can't tell you all that we have learned with cassini .	痛苦我無法告訴你們 , 我們從柬ssini身上學到 。

so i'm going to concentrate on two of the most exciting stories that have emerged out of this major exploratory expedition that we are conducting around saturn , and have been for the past two and a half years .	接下來我要和大家分享最令人興奮的故事之一 , 我們在兩年半年來 , 一直在過去兩年半年 。
saturn is accompanied by a very large and diverse collection of moons .	土星是非常大且多樣化的收藏物 。
they range in size from a few kilometers across to as big across as the u . s .	他們從幾公里遠距離幾公里的距離 , 來到大規模 。

now , two of the 47 moons that saturn has are standouts .	現在 , 土星總共有247個月球 。
and those are titan and enceladus . titan is saturn's largest moon , and , until cassini had arrived there , was the largest single expanse of unexplored terrain that we had remaining in our solar system .	這些是土星和土衛二 , 直到克里斯達那裡 , 這是我們太陽系中最大的最大規模之一 。
and it is a body that has long intrigued people who've watched the planets .	它是個身體 , 有很長的親密關係 , 讓大家看過地球 。
it has a very large , thick atmosphere , and in fact , its surface environment was believed to be more like the environment we have here on the earth , or at least had in the past , than any other body in the solar system .	它有著巨大的大氣層 , 在地球上 , 至少在過去 , 比任何其他身體都在太陽系中 。
its atmosphere is largely molecular nitrogen , like you are breathing here in this room , except that its atmosphere is suffused with simple organic materials like methane and propane and ethane .	大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 大氣層是大氣層 , 像是甲烷、甲烷、乙烷 。
and these molecules high up in the atmosphere of titan get broken down , and their products join together to make haze particles .	這些分子在大氣層的大氣中被破壞 , 而他們的產品加入了大氣層 , 將它們的混合物結合起來 。
this haze is ubiquitous . it's completely global and enveloping titan .	這種仇恨是完全全球性的 , 完全是全球性的 。
and that's why you cannot see down to the surface with our eyes in the visible region of the spectrum .	這就是為什麼你無法在眼睛看到這個光譜的區域 。
but these haze particles , it was surmised , before we got there with cassini , over billions and billions of years , gently drifted down to the surface and coated the surface in a thick organic sludge .	但這些海岸的微粒子 , 經過幾十億年的時間 , 經過數十億年的時間 , 將水平面上升到水面上 , 經過幾十億年的時間 , 讓水平面積極度地融化 。
so like the equivalent , the titan equivalent , of tar , or oil , or what we didn't know what .	所以 , 像是水準、油、或石油 , 我們不知道什麼 。
but this is what we suspected . and these molecules , especially methane and ethane , can be liquids at the surface temperatures of titan .	但這是我們所懷疑的 。 這些分子 , 特別甲烷和甲烷 , 可以是甲烷和甲烷的表面 。
and so it turns out that methane is to titan what water is to the earth .	結果發現 , 甲烷是土地的甲烷 。
it's a condensable in the atmosphere , and so recognizing this circumstance brought to the fore a whole world of bizarre possibilities . you can have methane clouds , ok , and above those clouds , you have this hundreds of kilometers of haze , which prevent any sunlight from getting to the surface .	它是大氣層的 , 可以有一百公里的大氣層 , 讓任何陽光照射到水面上 。
the temperature at the surface is some 350 degrees below zero fahrenheit .	表面的溫度是350度 , 表面的溫度是350度 。
but despite that cold , you could have rain falling down on the surface of titan .	但儘管如此寒冷 , 你可以雨下降落在土地上 。
and doing on titan what rain does on the earth: it carves gullies ; it forms rivers and cataracts ; it can create canyons ; it can pool in large basins and craters .	在地球上 , 它可以形成河流和洞穴 ; 它可以形成河流和洞穴 ; 它可以形成河流和洞穴 , 它可以形成河流和洞穴 。
it can wash the sludge off high mountain peaks and hills , down into the lowlands . so stop and think for a minute .	它可以用高山脈衝擊 , 到低地 , 直到下降 , 下降到低地 , 所以停下來想想 。

it's dark . high noon on titan is as dark as deep earth twilight on the earth .	它是黑暗的 , 深在地球上的黑暗 。

that is the view that we had of the surface of titan before we got there with cassini , and i can tell you that what we have found on titan , though it is not the same in detail , is every bit as fascinating as that story is .	這是我們在titan所看到的 , 我們在泰坦的表面上看到了什麼 , 我們在泰坦的表面上發現了 , 雖然它不是同樣的細節 , 但它還不一樣 。

but anyway , the probe took measurements of the atmosphere on the way down , and it also took panoramic pictures .	不管如何 , 它也引起了大氣層的大氣層 , 它也拍攝了大氣層 。

it is a very geologically active body .	它是非常地活性的身體 。
but the mother lode of discoveries on enceladus was found at the south pole and we're looking at the south pole here where we found this system of fractures .	但在南極 , 我們發現的是南極 , 我們發現在南極地區 , 我們發現了這個系統 。
and they're a different color because they're a different composition .	它們是不同的顏色 , 因為它們是不同的顏色 。
they are coated . these fractures are coated with organic materials .	它們被覆蓋 , 這些碎片是有機物質 。
moreover , this whole , entire region , the south polar region , has elevated temperatures . it's the hottest place on the planet , on the body .	此外 , 整個區域 , 南極區域 , 它是地球上最熱的地方 。
that's as bizarre as finding that the antarctic on the earth is hotter than the tropics .	這很奇怪 , 地球上的北極圈是熱帶的 。
and then , when we took additional pictures , we discovered that from these fractures are issuing jets of fine , icy particles extending hundreds of miles into space .	接著 , 當我們拍攝時 , 我們發現從這些碎片中有數百英哩 , 進入太空中 。
and when we colorcode this image , to bring out the faint light levels , we see that these jets feed a plume that , in fact , we see , in other images , goes thousands of miles into the space above enceladus .	當我們把這張圖片放進到太空中 , 我們看到這些噴射的光線 , 我們會看到這些噴射的光線 , 數以千計的速度 。
my team and i have examined images like this , and like this one , and have thought about the other results from cassini .	我的團隊和我的研究結果發現 , 像這樣 , 像這樣 , 像這樣 , 像這樣 , 像這樣 , 來看看其他的結果 。
and we have arrived at the conclusion that these jets may be erupting from pockets of liquid water under the surface of enceladus .	我們已經得到了結論 , 這些猶太人可能在土地表面放棄 , 把液態水放在水底下 。
so we have , possibly , liquid water , organic materials and excess heat .	所以 , 我們有有機物質、有機物質、有機物質 , 及冰川 。
in other words , we have possibly stumbled upon the holy grail of modern day planetary exploration , or in other words , an environment that is potentially suitable for living organisms .	換句話說 , 我們可能在現代天星探索的環境中 , 或其他文字中 , 生命有機體存在的可能性 。
and i don't think i need to tell you that the discovery of life elsewhere in our solar system , whether it be on enceladus or elsewhere , would have enormous cultural and scientific implications .	我不認為我需要告訴各位 , 在我們的太陽系中發現了其他地方 , 它會有巨大的文化和科學領域 。
because if we could demonstrate that genesis had occurred not once , but twice , independently , in our solar system , then that means , by inference , it has occurred a staggering number of times throughout the universe and its 13 . 7 billion year history .	因為如果我們能證明 , 基因發生了什麼事 , 但 , 兩次 , 總體來說 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 它已經發生了很大的差異 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 它已經發生了 , 不久後 , 它已經發生了幾次 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 它已經發生了幾次 , 在我們的太陽系中 。
right now , earth is the only planet still that we know is teeming with life .	現在 , 地球是唯一的星球 , 地球是我們知道的生命 。
it is precious , it is unique , it is still , so far , the only home we've ever known .	它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 , 它很珍貴 。
and if any of you were alert and coherent during the 1960s and we'd forgive you , if you weren't , ok you would remember this very famous picture taken by the apollo 8 astronauts in 1968 .	如果你們在1968年到1968年被阿波羅飛行器拍攝 , 會記得這個非常有名的照片 。
it was the first time that earth was imaged from space , and it had an enormous impact on our sense of place in the universe , and our sense of responsibility for the protection of our own planet .	這是第一次 , 地球上有著巨大的衝擊 , 我們對於地球的信任感知 , 對於我們對於地球的保護 , 我們的感覺非常巨大 。
well , we on cassini have taken an equivalent first , a picture that no human eye has ever seen before .	嗯 , 我們在加薩斯林的第一張照片 , 人類眼睛已經見過 。
it is a total eclipse of the sun , seen from the other side of saturn .	它是太陽的一面 , 來自土星的一面 。
and in this impossibly beautiful picture , you see the main rings backlit by the sun , you see the refracted image of the sun and you see this ring created , in fact , by the exhalations of enceladus .	在這張圖片中 , 你看到了這張圖片的圖片 , 你看到了這張相片的圖片 , 你看到了這張圖片 , 正是太陽的影像 , 你看到了這張相片的圖片 。
but as if that weren't brilliant enough , we can spot , in this beautiful image , sight of our own planet , cradled in the arms of saturn's rings .	但如果那不夠精彩 , 我們就能在地球上 , 在這個美麗的影像中 , 以我們的星球的角度來看 , 像我們自己的星球一樣 。
now , there is something deeply moving about seeing ourselves from afar , and capturing the sight of our little , blueocean planet in the skies of other worlds .	現在 , 我們有一些深刻的看法 , 把我們的小小、藍色星球和其他世界各地的相互作用 。
and that , and the perspective of ourselves that we gain from that , may be , in the end , the finest reward that we earn from this journey of discovery that started half a century ago .	而我們從這段旅程中發現的最佳獎勵 , 就是我們從這個旅程中發現的一世紀前 。
as of 2005 , only 15 percent of the world was mapped . this slows the delivery of aid after a disaster and hides the economic potential of unused lands and unknown roads . in this short talk , google's lalitesh katragadda demos map maker , a group mapmaking tool that people around the globe are using to map their world .	2005年 , 只有15%的人口在全球各地地圖上 , 用地圖來製造r , 全球各地地圖製造者 , 一群地圖製造者 , 一群地圖製造者 , 全球各地地圖製造者 , 一個團隊地圖製造者 , 一個團隊地圖製造者 , 全球各地地圖製造者 。

nobel prize nominee hernando de soto recognized that the key to economic liftoff for most developing countries is to tap the vast amounts of uncapitalized land .	諾貝爾獎得主 , 諾貝爾獎得主席 , 大部分開發中國家都要用大量的金融化土地 。

in the last year alone , thousands of users in 170 countries have mapped millions of pieces of information , and created a map of a level of detail never thought viable .	去年 , 數以千計的數以百萬計的資料庫裡 , 創造了一百個字母 , 以數以千計的使用者 , 創造出一個完全不可思議的地圖 。

in 2003 , the palestinian village of budrus mounted a 10monthlong nonviolent protest to stop a barrier being built across their olive groves . did you hear about it ? didn't think so . brazilian filmmaker julia bacha asks why we only pay attention to violence in the israelpalestine conflict and not to the nonviolent leaders who may one day bring peace .	在2003年 , 巴西亞•巴西的穆斯林•巴西斯•巴西斯•布達德魯斯打造出一個10個月大的抗議 , 來阻止阻止阻止障礙發生的暴力領袖 , 而非暴力的領導者 , 會問為什麼我們只關注暴力的領導者 , 而不是去做暴力的領袖 , 會問為什麼我們唯一關注暴力的領導者 。
arts , communication , compassion , entertainment , film , peace , violence , war	藝術、溝通 , 和平、暴力、戰爭 , 和平、暴力、戰爭 。
julia bacha: pay attention to nonviolence	朱利亞:注意到非暴力行為 。
for the last 8 years , i have dedicated my life to documenting the work of israelis and palestinians who are trying to end the conflict using peaceful means .	過去8年來 , 我一直在嘗試終止衝突與巴勒斯坦人在試圖終止衝突與巴勒斯坦人合作 。
when i travel with my work across europe and the united states , one question always comes up: where is the palestinian gandhi ?	當我在歐洲和美國一起旅行時 , 一個問題總是會出現:那是巴勒斯坦甘地嗎 ?
why aren't palestinians using nonviolent resistance ?	為什麼不是巴勒斯坦人用非暴力抗拒 ?
the challenge i face when i hear this question is that often i have just returned from the middle east where i spent my time filming dozens of palestinians who are using nonviolence to defend their lands and water resources from israeli soldiers and settlers .	當我聽到這問題時 , 我聽到的問題是 , 當我聽到這問題時 , 我花了幾年的時間拍攝幾十位巴勒斯坦人 , 他們用非暴力來防禦他們的土地和水資源 , 來自以色列士兵和水資源來保護他們的土地 。
these leaders are trying to forge a massive national nonviolent movement to end the occupation and build peace in the region .	這些領導者試圖將大規模國家的暴力運動結合在一起 , 並建立和平 。
yet , most of you have probably never heard about them .	然而 , 你們當中大多數人可能從來沒有聽過他們 。
this divide between what's happening on the ground and perceptions abroad is one of the key reasons why we don't have yet a palestinian peaceful resistance movement that has been successful .	在地面和平面上發生了什麼事 , 和平的抗議性運動已經成功了 。
so i'm here today to talk about the power of attention , the power of your attention , and the emergence and development of nonviolent movements in the west bank , gaza and elsewhere but today , my case study is going to be palestine .	今天我要講的是關於注意力的力量 , 你注意力的力量 , 在西方銀行、加薩和其他地方 , 但現在 , 我的案例研究將會是巴勒斯坦 。
i believe that what's mostly missing for nonviolence to grow is not for palestinians to start adopting nonviolence , but for us to start paying attention to those who already are .	我相信 , 最糟糕的是 , 非暴力行為 , 而是為了我們開始對抗暴力 , 但對我們而言 , 要開始做非暴力的事 , 而是讓我們開始對抗非暴力的行為 。
allow me to illustrate this point by taking you to this village called budrus .	讓我來說明一下這個村莊 , 叫做布德魯斯 。
about seven years ago , they faced extinction , because israel announced it would build a separation barrier , and part of this barrier would be built on top of the village .	大約七年前 , 他們面臨殺害 , 因為以色列宣佈 , 它會建構在村莊的一部分 。
they would lose 40 percent of their land and be surrounded , so they would lose free access to the rest of the west bank .	他們會損失40%的土地 , 所以他們會損失40%的土地 , 所以他們會損失40%的土地 , 所以他們會失去自由 。
through inspired local leadership , they launched a peaceful resistance campaign to stop that from happening .	透過啟發了和平的抗議 , 他們發出了一個和平的抗議活動 , 來阻止發生發生 。
let me show you some brief clips , so you have a sense for what that actually looked like on the ground .	讓我給你們看一些短片 , 所以你有某種程度的感覺 , 像是在地面上 。

here in budrus , we realized the wall would steal our land .	在布德魯斯 , 我們意識到牆會偷我們的土地 。

julia bacha: when i first heard about the story of budrus , i was surprised that the international media had failed to cover the extraordinary set of events that happened seven years ago , in 2003 .	朱利亞•巴卡:當我第一次聽到關於布德魯的故事時 , 我很驚訝 , 在2003年 , 國際媒體已經失敗了 。
what was even more surprising was the fact that budrus was successful .	更令人驚訝的是 , 布德魯斯成功了 。
the residents , after 10 months of peaceful resistance , convinced the israeli government to move the route of the barrier off their lands and to the green line , which is the internationally recognized boundary between israel and the palestinian territories .	數十個月後 , 阿拉伯人與巴勒斯坦人一起走路 , 將他們的土地轉換成綠線 , 以色列為南方 , 以色列政府向外向南方 , 將它們土地轉換成綠線 , 以色列為基礎 。
the resistance in budrus has since spread to villages across the west bank and to palestinian neighborhoods in jerusalem .	巴勒斯坦的鄰居在耶路撒冷 , 巴勒斯坦街坊在耶路撒冷 。
yet the media remains mostly silent on these stories .	但媒體仍然在這些故事中很沉默 。
this silence carries profound consequences for the likelihood that nonviolence can grow , or even survive , in palestine .	這種沉默的後果很可能會長大 , 或甚至生存 , 在巴勒斯坦 。
violent resistance and nonviolent resistance share one very important thing in common ; they are both a form of theater seeking an audience to their cause .	暴力抗爭和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗拒性和非暴力抗藥性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗藥性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗藥性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗抗性和非暴力抗藥性 ,
if violent actors are the only ones constantly getting frontpage covers and attracting international attention to the palestinian issue , it becomes very hard for nonviolent leaders to make the case to their communities that civil disobedience is a viable option in addressing their plight .	如果暴力的選舉是唯一的一員 , 才能讓暴力的領袖去做這個案例 , 讓暴力的領袖們成為他們所謂的 「 暴力者 」 , 才能讓這個案例成為 「 暴力者 」 , 讓暴力的領袖能夠讓他們成為 「 暴力者 」 , 讓他們成為 「 暴力者 」 , 讓他們成為 「 暴力者 」 。
the power of attention is probably going to come as no surprise to the parents in the room .	注意力的注意力可能會發生在房間裡 。
the surest way to make your child throw increasingly louder tantrums is by giving him attention the first time he throws a fit .	要讓你的孩子變得更加強大 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強大 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強大 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強大 , 讓你的孩子變得更加強烈地追求 。
the tantrum will become what childhood psychologists call a functional behavior , since the child has learned that he can get parental attention out of it .	tantrum會成為兒童心理學家稱之為功能性行為 , 因為孩子們知道他可以把注意力分開 。
parents can incentivize or disincentivize behavior simply by giving or withdrawing attention to their children .	父母可以激勵或把注意力放在他們的孩子身上 。
but that's true for adults too .	但對成年人也是如此 。
in fact , the behavior of entire communities and countries can be influenced , depending on where the international community chooses to focus its attention .	事實上 , 整個社區的行為 , 都會影響到國際社群的行為 , 讓國際社群選擇聚焦注意力 。
i believe that at the core of ending the conflict in the middle east and bringing peace is for us to transform nonviolence into a functional behavior by giving a lot more attention to the nonviolent leaders on the ground today .	我相信 , 在中東和平 , 要讓我們改變非暴力的領導者 , 來改變非暴力的領導者 。
in the course of taking my film to villages in the west bank , in gaza and in east jerusalem , i have seen the impact that even one documentary film can have in influencing the transformation .	在加薩和東耶路撒冷 , 我看到了這部電影的影響 , 甚至一部電影可以影響到這個轉變 。
in a village called wallajeh , which sits very close to jerusalem , the community was facing a very similar plight to budrus .	在一個村莊裡 , 一個叫做牆拉jeh的村莊 , 非常接近耶路撒冷 , 社區正面臨著非常類似的飛行 。
they were going to be surrounded , lose a lot of their lands and not have freedom of access , either to the west bank or jerusalem .	他們會被摧毀 , 失去了許多土地 , 沒有自由 , 或耶路撒冷 。
they had been using nonviolence for about two years but had grown disenchanted since nobody was paying attention .	兩年來 , 沒有人會注意到 , 因為沒有人會注意 。
so we organized a screening .	所以我們組織了一張螢幕 。
a week later , they held the most wellattended and disciplined demonstration to date .	一週後 , 他們重建了最好的目標 , 和破壞了 。
the organizers say that the villagers , upon seeing the story of budrus documented in a film , felt that there were indeed people following what they were doing , that people cared .	組織者說 , 村民們在電影裡看到了關於布德魯斯的故事 , 在電影中看到了關於布德魯斯的故事 , 人們會在電影中看到他們正在做的事 , 人們會在乎他們在做的事 。
so they kept on going .	所以他們繼續繼續下去 。
on the israeli side , there is a new peace movement called solidariot , which means solidarity in hebrew .	以色列為基礎 , 有一種新的和平運動叫做 「 蘇格蘭德 」 , 意思是 「 蘇格蘭人 」 。
the leaders of this movement have been using budrus as one of their primary recruiting tools .	這項運動的領導者正在使用布德魯斯 , 其中一個主要的招募工具之一 。
they report that israelis who had never been active before , upon seeing the film , understand the power of nonviolence and start joining their activities .	他們報導了非暴力的力量 , 開始加入他們的活動 。
the examples of wallajeh and the solidariot movement show that even a smallbudget independent film can play a role in transforming nonviolence into a functional behavior .	和蘇格蘭運動的例子 , 即使非暴力行為發生在改變非暴力的行為中 。
now imagine the power that big media players could have if they started covering the weekly nonviolent demonstrations happening in villages like bil'in , ni'lin , wallajeh , in jerusalem neighborhoods like sheikh jarrah and silwan the nonviolent leaders would become more visible , valued and effective in their work .	現在 , 想像一下 , 大媒體玩家的力量會變得更有價值 , 並且有效地在他們工作中所做的事 , 像是布爾瓦 , 巴爾 , 巴爾 , 巴爾 , 非暴力的暴力行為 。
i believe that the most important thing is to understand that if we don't pay attention to these efforts , they are invisible , and it's as if they never happened .	我相信最重要的事情是要了解如果我們不把注意力投入這些努力 , 他們就會隱形 , 不管他們是怎麼看待的 。
but i have seen first hand that if we do , they will multiply .	但是我第一次手到如果我們這麼做 , 他們會多次 。
if they multiply , their influence will grow in the overall israelipalestinian conflict .	如果他們多次 , 他們的影響會成長在巴勒斯坦衝突中 。
and theirs is the kind of influence that can finally unblock the situation .	他們的影響力可以終於阻止這個情況 。
these leaders have proven that nonviolence works in places like budrus .	這些領導者證明了非暴力工作 , 像是佛羅斯 。
let's give them attention so they can prove it works everywhere .	我們給他們注意力 , 讓他們能證明它的工作 。
simon sinek has a simple but powerful model for inspirational leadership all starting with a golden circle and the question " why ? " his examples include apple , martin luther king , and the wright brothers . . .	西蒙斯坦克有個簡單的例子 , 包括蘋果、馬丁•路德•金恩 , 和 「 為什麼 ? 」 他的例子包括蘋果、馬丁•路德•金恩 , 和 「 為什麼 ? 」
bullseye , business , entrepreneur , leadership , sales , selling , success	商業、商業、企業家、領導力、財富、企業、商業、企業家、領導力、銷售、成功 。
simon sinek: how great leaders inspire action	sinek:偉大的領導者鼓勵行動 。
how do you explain when things don't go as we assume ?	你要如何解釋當我們假設不存在時 , 會怎麼解釋 ?
or better , how do you explain when others are able to achieve things that seem to defy all of the assumptions ?	或更好的是 , 你怎麼解釋其他人能夠達到這些假設 ?
for example: why is apple so innovative ?	舉例來說:為什麼蘋果這麼創新 ?
year after year , after year , after year , they're more innovative than all their competition .	一年後 , 一年後 , 他們比所有競爭都更創新 。
and yet , they're just a computer company .	然而 , 他們只是一個電腦公司 。
they're just like everyone else .	他們就像其他人一樣 。
they have the same access to the same talent , the same agencies , the same consultants , the same media .	他們有相同的成果 , 同樣的媒體 , 相同的顧問 , 同樣的媒體 。
then why is it that they seem to have something different ?	為什麼他們似乎有不同的東西 ?
why is it that martin luther king led the civil rights movement ?	為什麼 , 馬丁路德金恩會把民權運動帶給民權運動 ?
he wasn't the only man who suffered in a precivil rights america , and he certainly wasn't the only great orator of the day .	他肯定不是唯一的男子 , 他肯定不是唯一的美國人 , 他肯定不是唯一的男人 。
and why is it that the wright brothers were able to figure out controlled , powered man flight when there were certainly other teams who were better qualified , better funded . . .	原因是 , 萊兄弟能夠找出控制權力 , 更好的資金 , 更好的資金 。
and they didn't achieve powered man flight , and the wright brothers beat them to it .	他們沒有達到權力的人飛行 , 雷兄兄弟打敗他們 。
there's something else at play here .	這裡還有其他的東西 。
about three and a half years ago i made a discovery .	三年半前 , 我做了一個發現 。
and this discovery profoundly changed my view on how i thought the world worked , and it even profoundly changed the way in which i operate in it .	這個發現深深地改變了我看待世界的方式 , 甚至徹底改變了我的觀念 。
as it turns out , there's a pattern .	結果發現 , 這是個模式 。
as it turns out , all the great and inspiring leaders and organizations in the world whether it's apple or martin luther king or the wright brothers they all think , act and communicate the exact same way .	結果發現 , 所有偉大、令人激勵的領導人和世界各地的領導者和組織 , 不論是蘋果或馬丁路德金 , 或馬丁•路德金 , 或瑪丁•路德金 , 或他們所有偉大的領導者 , 都可以用同樣的方式來溝通 。
and it's the complete opposite to everyone else .	完全相反對其他人來說 。
all i did was codify it , and it's probably the world's simplest idea .	我所做的是 , 它可能是世界上最簡單的想法 。
i call it the golden circle .	我稱它為黃金圈 。
why ? how ? what ?	為什麼 ? 為什麼 ?
this little idea explains why some organizations and some leaders are able to inspire where others aren't .	這個小點子解釋了為什麼有些組織和一些領導者能夠啟發他人不存在 。
let me define the terms really quickly .	讓我定義這個詞很快 。
every single person , every single organization on the planet knows what they do , 100 percent .	每個人 , 每個組織都知道他們所做的事 , 100% 。
some know how they do it , whether you call it your differentiated value proposition or your proprietary process or your usp .	有些人知道他們如何做 , 不論你稱它為 「 不論你是如何做 」 或你的複製品 , 或你的複製過程 。
but very , very few people or organizations know why they do what they do .	但 , 非常少人或組織知道為什麼他們會這麼做 。
and by " why " i don't mean " to make a profit . "	「 為何 」 我不代表 「 為何 」 的意思 。
that's a result . it's always a result .	這是結果 , 結果是結果 。
by " why , " i mean: what's your purpose ?	「 為什麼 ? 」 我的意思是 , 你的目的是什麼 ?
what's your cause ? what's your belief ?	你的信念是什麼 ? 你的信念是什麼 ?
why does your organization exist ?	為什麼你的組織存在 ?
why do you get out of bed in the morning ?	為什麼你早上早上起床呢 ?
and why should anyone care ?	為什麼要有人關心 ?
well , as a result , the way we think , the way we act , the way we communicate is from the outside in .	結果是 , 我們所做的 , 就是從外面來看 。
it's obvious . we go from the clearest thing to the fuzziest thing .	很明顯 , 我們從最明顯的角度來看 , 很明顯 。
but the inspired leaders and the inspired organizations regardless of their size , regardless of their industry all think , act and communicate from the inside out .	但鼓舞的領導者和靈感組織 , 不管他們的產業都在想 , 和激勵的組織 , 不管他們在做什麼 , 不論是如何 。
let me give you an example .	讓我舉個例子 。
i use apple because they're easy to understand and everybody gets it .	我使用蘋果 , 因為他們很容易理解 , 每個人都能理解 。
if apple were like everyone else , a marketing message from them might sound like this: " we make great computers .	如果蘋果跟其他人一樣 , 市場訊息會聽起來像這樣: 「 我們製造很棒的電腦 。
they're beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	它們很漂亮 , 簡單使用和使用者友善 。
want to buy one ? " " meh . "	想買一個 ? 「 啊 ! 」
and that's how most of us communicate .	那就是我們大部分人溝通的方式 。
that's how most marketing is done , that's how most sales is done and that's how most of us communicate interpersonally .	這是最多的銷售量 , 最多的銷售量是最多的 , 這是大部分的銷售方式 。
we say what we do , we say how we're different or how we're better and we expect some sort of a behavior , a purchase , a vote , something like that .	我們會說我們怎麼做 , 我們會說我們如何做 , 我們會說我們如何做 , 我們會說我們如何做 , 我們會說我們是如何做的事 , 或更好的 , 我們會說我們是如何做的事 , 或更好的 , 我們會說我們是如何做的事 , 或我們如何更好 。
here's our new law firm: we have the best lawyers with the biggest clients , we always perform for our clients who do business with us .	這是我們的新法律:我們有最好的律師 , 我們有最好的律師 , 最好的律師 , 我們都有最好的律師 。
here's our new car: it gets great gas mileage , it has leather seats , buy our car .	這是我們的車:它有了大氣體 , 一輛車子 , 可以買我們的車 。
here's how apple actually communicates .	這是蘋果如何溝通 。
" everything we do , we believe in challenging the status quo .	「 我們所做的一切 , 我們相信有挑戰性的地位 。
we believe in thinking differently .	我們相信在思考不同 。
the way we challenge the status quo is by making our products beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	我們挑戰的方式 , 就是讓產品設計很簡單 , 使用和使用者友善 。
we just happen to make great computers .	我們只是為了製造偉大的電腦 。
want to buy one ? "	想要買一個嗎 ? 」
totally different right ? you're ready to buy a computer from me .	完全不同 ? 你準備好要買一台電腦 。
all i did was reverse the order of the information .	我所做的就是把資訊傳遞給資訊 。
what it proves to us is that people don't buy what you do ; people buy why you do it .	這證明了我們是人們不買你做的事 , 人們買了你做的事 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做的事 , 他們買了你做的事 。
this explains why every single person in this room is perfectly comfortable buying a computer from apple .	這解釋為什麼每個人在這個房間裡每個人都很自用蘋果 。
but we're also perfectly comfortable buying an mp3 player from apple , or a phone from apple , or a dvr from apple .	但我們也非常舒適地購買一個來自蘋果的dvr , 或來自蘋果公司的手機 , 或來自蘋果公司的手機 。
but , as i said before , apple's just a computer company .	但 , 如同我之前說的 , 蘋果只是電腦公司 。
there's nothing that distinguishes them structurally from any of their competitors .	沒有任何事故障礙他們的競爭者 。
their competitors are all equally qualified to make all of these products .	他們的競爭者都平等地做這些產品 。
in fact , they tried .	事實上 , 他們嘗試了 。
a few years ago , gateway came out with flat screen tvs .	幾年前 , 格雷特•雷特發出了廣播電視 。
they're eminently qualified to make flat screen tvs .	他們很高興能創造出廣泛的電視 。
they've been making flat screen monitors for years .	數年來 , 他們已經製造了廣泛的螢幕 。
dell came out with mp3 players and pdas , and they make great quality products , and they can make perfectly welldesigned products and nobody bought one .	迪爾從三位玩家和pda玩家 , 他們製作了很棒品質產品 , 他們製造了很棒的品質產品 , 他們製造了很棒的品質產品 , 然後他們製造出很好的品質產品 , 並且他們能做出完美的產品 , 且他們能做出完美的產品 。
in fact , talking about it now , we can't even imagine buying an mp3 player from dell .	事實上 , 談到現在 , 我們甚至無法想像購買一個mp3玩家 。
why would you buy an mp3 player from a computer company ?	為什麼你會買一台電腦公司的一台電腦公司 ?
but we do it every day .	但我們每天都這麼做 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做的事 , 他們買了你做的事 。
the goal is not to do business with everybody who needs what you have .	目標不是要做任何事業 , 需要你有的人 。
the goal is to do business with people who believe what you believe .	目標是要和那些相信你相信的人 。
here's the best part: none of what i'm telling you is my opinion .	最好的部分是:我對你們說的不是我所說的 。
it's all grounded in the tenets of biology .	它是生物學的基礎 。
not psychology , biology .	不是心理學、生物學 。
if you look at a crosssection of the human brain , looking from the top down , what you see is the human brain is actually broken into three major components that correlate perfectly with the golden circle .	如果你仔細觀察人類大腦的功能 , 將它轉換成三個主要的組合 , 與黃金圓圈相互作用 。
our newest brain , our homo sapien brain , our neocortex , corresponds with the " what " level .	我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 , 我們的大腦 。
the neocortex is responsible for all of our rational and analytical thought and language .	新皮層是負責我們所有理性、分析思想和語言的方式 。
the middle two sections make up our limbic brains , and our limbic brains are responsible for all of our feelings , like trust and loyalty .	中間的兩個部份會讓我們的腦部有責任 , 我們的肢體大腦有責任 , 我們的肢體大腦有責任 , 我們的肢體大腦有責任 , 我們的肢體大腦有責任 , 我們的肢體大腦都是負責任的 。
it's also responsible for all human behavior , all decisionmaking , and it has no capacity for language .	它也對所有人類行為、決策都有責任 , 也沒有任何能力 。
in other words , when we communicate from the outside in , yes , people can understand vast amounts of complicated information like features and benefits and facts and figures .	換句話說 , 當我們溝通到外面時 , 人們可以理解大量複雜的資訊 , 像是特徵、有益、事實和事實 。
it just doesn't drive behavior .	它不動行為 。
when we can communicate from the inside out , we're talking directly to the part of the brain that controls behavior , and then we allow people to rationalize it with the tangible things we say and do .	當我們能從外面傳遞到大腦的控制行為時 , 我們就會直接傳遞到大腦控制行為的部分 , 然後讓我們讓大家能用我們所說的最佳的方式來處理 。
this is where gut decisions come from .	這是猜決定來自哪裡 。
you know , sometimes you can give somebody all the facts and figures , and they say , " i know what all the facts and details say , but it just doesn't feel right . "	你知道 , 有時候你可以給某人的事實和細節 , 他們說: 「 我知道所有的事實和細節 , 但那只是不合理 。 」
why would we use that verb , it doesn't " feel " right ?	為什麼我們會用這個字詞 , 不是 「 感覺 」 是的 ?
because the part of the brain that controls decisionmaking doesn't control language .	因為大腦的一部分是控制決策 , 控制決策不控制 。
and the best we can muster up is , " i don't know . it just doesn't feel right . "	最好的就是: 「 我不知道 , 感覺不好 。 」
or sometimes you say you're leading with your heart , or you're leading with your soul .	有時候你會引起你的心靈 , 或者你是你的心靈魂 。
well , i hate to break it to you , those aren't other body parts controlling your behavior .	嗯 , 我討厭破壞它 , 那些不是其他身體的部分控制你的行為 。
it's all happening here in your limbic brain , the part of the brain that controls decisionmaking and not language .	它在你的腦袋裡發生了 , 大腦控制決策和非語言 。
but if you don't know why you do what you do , and people respond to why you do what you do , then how will you ever get people to vote for you , or buy something from you , or , more importantly , be loyal and want to be a part of what it is that you do .	但如果你不知道為什麼你會這樣做 , 你就會做些什麼 , 然後人們會選擇你做的事 , 或更重要的是 , 去投票給你 , 或者 , 更重要的是 , 你會怎麼做 。
again , the goal is not just to sell to people who need what you have ; the goal is to sell to people who believe what you believe .	同樣的 , 目標是要賣給那些相信你的人 , 目標是要賣給那些相信你的人 。
the goal is not just to hire people who need a job ; it's to hire people who believe what you believe .	目標不只是要僱用工作 , 而是要僱用那些相信你相信的人 。
i always say that , you know , if you hire people just because they can do a job , they'll work for your money , but if you hire people who believe what you believe , they'll work for you with blood and sweat and tears .	我總是說 , 你知道嗎 ? 如果你僱用人 , 他們會為你的錢做工作 , 但如果你僱用那些相信你的人 , 他們會為你付錢 , 如果你僱用人 , 他們會為你的錢做工作 , 但如果你僱用這些人 , 他們會為你的錢做工作 , 但如果你僱用那些相信你的人 , 他們會為你的錢做工作 。
and nowhere else is there a better example of this than with the wright brothers .	另外還有一個更好的例子 , 比起更好的例子 。
most people don't know about samuel pierpont langley .	大部分的人都不知道西班牙語 。
and back in the early 20th century , the pursuit of powered man flight was like the dot com of the day .	回到20世紀初期 , 權力飛行的主動人飛行就像是日子的飛行 。
everybody was trying it .	每個人都在嘗試它 。
and samuel pierpont langley had , what we assume , to be the recipe for success .	samuelpontlangley , 我們所假設的 , 是成功的成功 。
i mean , even now , you ask people , " why did your product or why did your company fail ? "	我的意思是 , 即使現在 , 你問人們: 「 為什麼你的公司失敗 ? 」
and people always give you the same permutation of the same three things: undercapitalized , the wrong people , bad market conditions .	人們總是給你同樣的三樣東西:下降 , 不錯的人 , 壞市場條件 。
it's always the same three things , so let's explore that .	它總是相同三件事 , 所以我們來探索 。
samuel pierpont langley was given 50 , 000 dollars by the war department to figure out this flying machine .	samuelpontlangley已經花了五萬美金 , 把這台飛機飛行機器 。
money was no problem .	錢沒有問題 。
he held a seat at harvard and worked at the smithsonian and was extremely wellconnected ; he knew all the big minds of the day .	他在哈佛大學和史密斯森林工作 , 他知道所有大心智 。
he hired the best minds money could find and the market conditions were fantastic .	他僱用最好的心智金錢能找到和市場條件很棒 。
the new york times followed him around everywhere , and everyone was rooting for langley .	紐約時報到各地 , 每個人都在找尋求 。
then how come we've never heard of samuel pierpont langley ?	那麼 , 我們從來沒有聽過samuelpontlangley ?
a few hundred miles away in dayton ohio , orville and wilbur wright , they had none of what we consider to be the recipe for success .	幾百英哩遠的地方 , 波爾•威爾威爾 , 他們沒有我們認為要成為成功的成功 。
